Blingken meeting Qin Gang analyzed: Provide an opportunity for alleviating the tension between the United States and China

Publisher: Radio Free Asia (Organization)

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T11:24:40-04:00

U.S. Secretary of State Brillings and Chinese State Commission and Foreign Minister Qin Gang shake hands to pay hands on the 18th before the talks. Audio-1-Link: https: //www.rfa.org/mandarin/yataibaodao/junshiwaijiao/hcm-0618202307543.html/@stream](https://www.rfa.org/mandarin/yataibaodao/junshiwaijiao/hcm-06182023075433.html/@@stream)U.S. Secretary of State Broskerer visited Beijing on June 18 and held talks with Chinese Foreign Minister Qin Gang. Brincken is the first supreme US official to visit China in five years. After the Chinese spy balloon incident in February this year, Brinken postponed the plan to visit. Some analysts believe that the meeting between Blint and Qin Gang has provided an opportunity to ease the tension between the United States and China.

International Organization calls on Brinkens to make account on Chinese human rights and the United States, and then you will be recruited * Bolling Kenkee's visit to China is an expert: the U.S. -China relations are difficult to change

Chinese Foreign Minister Qin Gang welcomed the United States Secretary of State AntonyBlinken at the Diaoyutai State Guest House on Sunday. Qin Gang stretched out his hand first. After a few seconds, Brinken would come to shake hands with Qin Gang. The two did not talk to the media after taking pictures, and entered the conference room for closed -door talks.

Blink's less than 48 hours of whirlwind visits is quite compact. In addition to meeting with Qin Gang, he will also talk to Wang Yi, director of the Central Foreign Affairs Office of the Politburo.

At the earlier media briefing meeting, US officials faded any expectations of major progress in Blingken's visit, and "it is unlikely to make breakthroughs in any major issue."

"The most important purpose of the United States is the 'meeting'. The meeting this time makes the senior management of both parties really sit face to face." Huang Jiezheng, an associate professor of the Institute of International Affairs and Strategy of Tamkang University in Taiwan, told this station that at least the above meeting represents the balloon incident. The controversy caused by this page temporarily turned over. He believes that the tension of the rising tension of the evil line of the United States and China has slightly slowed down, and "this trip provides an opportunity to ease bilateral tension."

"With the continued tension of relations in the United States and China, the United States can build a pipeline of communication dialogue to the greatest extent, establish a mechanism for crisis management or risk avoidance." Song Guocheng, a researcher at the National Guan Center of Politburo in Taiwan, said This is the subjective expectation of the United States in China, but it does not mean that the United States shows weakness or reduces the siege of the CCP. The United States wants to "compete without confrontation."

布林肯周日清晨抵达北京，中国外交部北美大洋洲司司长杨涛与美国驻中大使伯恩斯到场迎接。(Reuters) The United States hopes to establish a channel for communication in China to avoid misjudgment

Earlier, Brinken has expressed three purposes to visit Beijing: one is to establish an open communication channel, deal with misunderstandings, and avoid misjudgment; The third is to explore cooperation space for issues such as stabilizing global economy and climate change.

On the other hand, Qin Gang talked to Bollingen in front of the meeting. According to the official release of China's officials, Qin Gang explained the strict position on the issues of China ’s core concerns such as Taiwan’ s issues, emphasizing that the United States should respect, stop interference in China ’s internal affairs, and stop harming the interests of Chinese sovereign security development in the name of competition.

Huang Jiezheng analyzed that the first item has done the first step. The outside world expects subsequent high -level officials including Janet Yellen, including US Finance Minister Janet Yellen and Commercial Secretary Ginaraimondo. consensus. However, he believes that it is difficult to reach the second item. "The United States must clearly state the value of the United States. Core in Beijing's core interests. "

Song Guocheng emphasized that "the United States and China are still structural confrontation", involving the competition for global leadership. The Chinese Communist Party attempts to compete for Asian hegemony and expel the US military existence to the global leadership of the United States and even replace the United States.

"Its ambitions have not changed at all. It is not to be the role of world peaceful builders. It must be the role of the world's highest leader. Isn't that the global leadership position, isn't it the point of the two strong resistance? "Song Guocheng added.

Blintken and Qin Gang held closed -door talks(Reuters) Biden: In the next few months, we will meet with Xi Jinping Huang Jiezheng analyzed that in November this year, the Asia -Pacific Economic Cooperation Conference (APEC) was sponsored by the United States. "The most important guest" Xi Jinping should not be absent. In addition, during the 20th National Group's Summit held in India this year, the leaders of the United States and China also had the opportunity to meet.

Song Guocheng pointed out that the only conclusion was "the next time for a while", but the substantial relationship between the United States and China has not improved. He said that from the perspective of Chinese military aircraft closer to the US military's approaching and rejection of the US -China military high -level dialogue, China did not show the sincerity of the dialogue.

Reporter: Huang Chunmei Responsible: Chen Meihua, Xu Shuting, He Ping.com Edited: Hong Wei

North Korea under the new crown epidemic: "We are trapped and waited for death"

North Korea under the new crown epidemic: "We are trapped and waited for death"

June 18, 2023 For several months, the BBC has been secretly contacted with three people in North Korea. They disclosed for the first time that the government blocked the disaster after blocking the border more than three years ago. Hunger and brutal suppression, but there is no chance to escape.

Ming Shu stared at the mobile phone with her body, fighting for the next sale. She is a savvy businessman who secretly sells smugglers to some urgent people with a small amount of supply, allowing her to live barely. She had been caught once, and it was reluctant to afford the dredging fee at that time before she was relieved.

She has almost no money to come again. However, knocking on the door may sound at any time. She was afraid of not only the police, but also her neighbors. Now she can hardly believe anyone. This is not the case. Mingshu's drug business was originally prosperous.

However, on January 27, 2020, North Korea suddenly closed the country to deal with the global epidemic. Citizens who have been banned from exporting are now closed in their own towns. Rescue workers and diplomats were packaged and left. The guards received the order, and any person near the border killed. The most isolated country in the world has become a black hole.

Under Kim Jong -un's totalitarian rule, North Korea was banned from contacting the outside world. With the help of the Northern Media "DailyNK" in the country in the country, the BBC was able to contact three North Korean civilians. They urgently want to tell the world about the catastrophic impact of Fengguan on their lives. They understand that if the government finds that they are reporting to us, they are likely to be executed. In order to protect them, we can only disclose what they tell us, but their experience provides a picture of rare domestic conditions in North Korea.

Mingshu

"Our food conditions have never been so bad," Ming Shu told us. Like most North Korean women, she is the main economic source of the family. The meager salary obtained from the mandatory government work is basically worthless, which forces their wives to come up with various ways to maintain their livelihood.

Before the closure, Ming Shu would find an urgent need of antibiotics such as antibiotics in various ways, stole them from China, and then sold them to their local market. She needs to buy the border guards, which occupies half of her profits, but she accepts the rules of the game. This allows her to live a comfortable life in the northern town that borders in China.

The burden of supporting her family has always given her heavy pressure, but now this pressure makes her overwhelmed. It is almost impossible to find a sellable product. On one occasion, she wanted to steal the drug by herself, but was caught. Now she is always surveillance. She tried to sell domestic drugs in North Korea, but it is difficult to find this now, and her income is almost halved.

Now, her husband and children wake up every day, and she will prepare corn breakfast for them. Her hungry neighbors have begun to knock on the door for food, but she has to reject them. "We all live on the edge of life," she said.

Chanhao

In another town of the border, the construction worker Chan Hao was frustrated the day in the morning. "I want people to know that I regret being born in this country," he vented like this.

He got up early, helped his wife to open the market, and then went to the construction site by himself. He did his best to help her move the goods and put it on the booth. He knew very well that he lived on her small business. He earns 4,000 North Korea -equivalent to $ 4 (£ 3) -the is not enough to buy a kilogram of rice, and his family has not received the government's grain for a long time, and he no longer expects.

He said that most North Koreans buying food markets are now almost empty, and the prices of rice, corn and seasonings have risen. Because the food produced by North Korea is not enough to be supplied to the citizens, it depends on imports. The blockade of the border allows the government to cut off the important food and fertilizers and machines for planting crops.

At the beginning, Chanhao was worried that he might die in the new crown, but over time, he began to worry about starving, especially after he watched the people around him died. The first to be starved to his village was a mother and her children. She was sick at the time. Her children rely on begging food to keep her life as much as possible, but in the end, all three died.

Then there was a mother who was sentenced to work because of violating the isolation order. She starved to death with her son. Recently, a acquaintance's son was released from the army because of malnutrition. Chanhao remembers that his face suddenly swelled, and then he died within a week. "I think of my children, thinking that we have to live in this unsatisfactory hell, and I can't sleep."

Hundreds of miles away, relatively rich capital Pyongyang, high -rise buildings on both sides of the rivers of the city. Zhiyan took the subway to work. After another sleepless night, she exhausted.

Her two children and husbands live on the money she earns in a food store. She once stole fruits and vegetables in the store to sell in the market, and she also sold cigarettes received by her husband from colleagues, and then bought rice with those money. Now, every time she get off work, the bag is thoroughly searched, and her husband no longer receives bribes. No one can afford anything.

"They have no longer possible," she was worried. Zhiyan now pretends to have three meals every day, but in fact she only eats one meal. She was hungry and was better than others knowing that she was poor.

She couldn't forget for a week, she was forced to eat "paste" -the food that mixed vegetables and grass into porridge into a paste. This food is inseparable from the darkest period in North Korea's history -in the 1990s devastating famine abused the country, causing as many as 3 million people to die.

"We all plan to survive 10 days in advance, and then plan for 10 days after the plan, thinking that if my husband and I are hungry, at least we can feed the children," Zhiyan said. Recently, she hasn't eaten for two days. "I thought I would die in my sleep, and I couldn't wake up in the morning," she said."This is a disaster," she said. "Without overseas supply, people don't know how to make a living." Recently, she heard that someone committed suicide at home, and some people hid in the mountains and died. She was distressed by the cold mentality of the city. "Even if someone dies next door, you will only think about yourself. It's so ruthless."

Image source, nk news

Image adding text,

During the new crown epidemic, the Pyongyang people wearing a mask are waiting for the train at an intersection.

For many months, the news of people's starving has been circulating, causing fear of may face another famine in North Korea. Peter Ward, an economist of North Korea, described the description of "very worrying".

"You heard that people starve to death are the same thing, but when you really know that the people around you are starving, this means that the food condition is very serious -worse than what we realize, and in the late 1990s The famine has been serious since any time, "he said.

North Korea's famine represents a turning point in the history of this country that is not long, causing its harsh social order to collapse. The government that cannot let people eat meals, give them fragmented freedom, and do what they need to do for life. Thousands of people fled out of the border and went to South Korea, Europe or the United States for refuge.

At the same time, the private market began to rise, and women began to sell soybeans, second -hand clothes and Chinese electronic products. A non -mainstream economy came into being, followed by a North Korean of the entire generation, and learned to make a living in the case of rarely helping the government -capitalists developed in a high -pressure communist country.

Image source, nk news

Image adding text,

Children in North Korea's famine in the 1990s

The market went to the building one day, and Ming Shu was calculating her revenue. She was worried that the government would start the capitalist generation for her and this capitalist generation. She believes that the global popularity is just an excuse for the authorities to re -control the people's lives. "Indeed, they want to fight smuggling and prevent people from escaping," she said. "Now, even if you are near the river near the Chinese border, you will be severely punished."

Construction worker Chanhao also reached the point of the collapse. This is the most difficult time he has experienced. The famine was difficult, he said, but at the time there was no such harsh suppression and punishment. "If people want to escape, the government can't do anything," he said. "Now, you may be executed in a wrong step."

His friend's son has recently witnessed the execution of the government several times. Three or four people were killed every time, and the charges were trying to escape. "If I live according to the rules, I am likely to starve to death, but as long as I try to escape, I am afraid that I may be arrested, the label as a traitor, and then to execute," Chanhao told us. "We are trapped here and wait for die."

In front of the border blockade, more than 1,000 escapers will arrive in South Korea each year, but after that, the number of people who are known to escape and reach South Korea is very small. Satellite pictures analyzed by Human Rightswatch (Human Rightswatch) show that the authorities have built many walls, fences and defense points along the border in the past three years, making it almost impossible to escape.

Just trying to contact foreign people is becoming more and more dangerous. In the past, residents near the border could also use mobile phones to be transported in from China to secretly call abroad through the mobile network of China Unicom. Now, Chanhao said that at each community party, people with Chinese mobile phones will be asked to surrender. Recently, a person he met by Ming Shu was discovered to call on the phone with the people in China, and was sentenced to several years.

Hannasong (transliteration) of the North Korean Human Rights Data Center (NKDB) said that by cracking down on smuggling and preventing people from contacting the outside world, the government is also depriving the people of the country to make a living. "When a grain is scarce, the government fully realizes what kind of damage this will cause," she said.

However, these extreme control measures cannot resist the new crown virus. On May 12, 2022, nearly two and a half years after the global popularity, North Korea officially confirmed its first confirmed case. Because there is no detection method, the people who have a fever are actually held at home for 10 days. The whole family will be prohibited from taking a step. As the epidemic spread, the town and the street were completely blocked, and sometimes it was more than two weeks.

In Pyongyang, Zhiyan looked at some neighbors out of her windows. They did not have enough food to adhere to the entire blockade period, and there was vegetables in front of them every day. But along the border, there is no help.

Ming Shu was panicked. Her life was already very tight, and the cabinets at home were empty. That's how she had to go crazy to sell medicine secretly. She felt the risk of getting sick to make money and starve to death.

Chanhao said that when the blockade was lifted, five families had "half dead". They only went out to find food after dark. "Those who stayed at home could not live," he said.

"People begged loudly, saying that they were starving to death, and for a few days, the government issued some rice from the inventory," he said. It is reported that the blockade in some areas has been lifted in advance, and people are obviously unable to survive if that.

Those infected people cannot rely on national ruined hospitals to treat them. Even the basic drugs are used up. The official suggestion is to use folk therapy to relieve symptoms. When Zhiyan became ill, he called his friends desperately. They suggested that she use boiling water to drink green onion.

According to Zhiyan, many elderly people and children died in the 2019 coronary virus. Health experts said that in a United Nations, 40%of countries with malnutrition of population are different from other countries, and children's infection is reasonable. A doctor in the city told Yan Yan that during the outbreak of the epidemic, every 550 people in Pyongyang died.

If it is calculated to the entire country, it is equivalent to more than 45,000 people, which is hundreds of times higher than the official announcement. But she got the news that everyone was informed of another cause of death, such as tuberculosis or liver cirrhosis.

In August 2022, three months after the outbreak of the epidemic, the government announced the victory of resistance, claiming that the virus had been cleared in China, but many isolation measures and regulations still took effect."I think those leaders have determined that the new crown virus can kill many people, at least the people who are not damaging, they are worried about those who will die," Peter Ward said. He refers to the army and elites that keep their power for the Jin family. There is one of the worst medical systems around the world. The overall population is malnourished and has not been vaccinated. Many people will die for a reasonable prediction.

But Song Hannah said that the new crown epidemic also gave Kim Jong Un a great opportunity to re -control people's lives. "This is what he wants to do secretly for a long time," she said. "His first priority has always been as much as possible to be isolated and controlled by his people."

separation

End of podcast

After making a little meager dinner, Zhiyan washed the dishes and cleaned her home. She climbed up to bed very early, hoping that she could rest better tonight. She will probably sleep more than Chanhao. The current work is very busy, and Chanhao often sleeps in the construction site.

However, in the relatively quiet border town of Ming Shu, she fell a little time, sitting with her family to watch TV, and used the battery that was charged during the day.

She especially likes watching Korean dramas, although these are prohibited. The show was sold and secretly sold through miniature SD cards. The latest episode that Ming Shu saw was about a K-Pop star appeared at the door of the family, claiming that he was his son who had been separated for many years. She said that since the border blockade, there are almost no new programs that can enter the border. In addition, the crackdown was very severe, and people became more careful.

She refers to the Reactionary Ideology and Culture RejectionAct adopted in December 2020. According to this law, people who smuggle foreign imaging products may be executed. Chanhao said that this is the "most terrible new law", and just watching these videos may face 10 years of imprisonment. According to the legal text obtained by "Daily North Korea", the purpose of the law is to prevent "a kind of decaying ideology that erodes our society".

Kim Jong -un's most worried thing is that his people understand the prosperous and free world outside their border, and wake up from the lies they hear.

Chanhao said that since the law was passed, foreign videos have almost disappeared. Only the younger generation dares to watch, which makes their parents extremely worried.

Zhiyan remembers a recent public trial in Pyongyang. Local leaders gathered together to judge a 22 -year -old man who shared Korean songs and movies. He was sentenced to 10 years and three months in the labor camp. Zhiyan said that before 2020, the trial of such cases usually only carried out quietly, and may be sentenced to one year in prison.

"The punishment is so much so much, and people are shocked," she said, "It's terrible, they are targeted at young people like this."

In 2019, former North Korean diplomat Ryu Hyun-Woo, a former North Korean diplomat, said that the formulation of the law is to ensure the loyalty of young people, because the attitude they developed is very different from their parents. "We have received a gift from the country since we were young, but under the leadership of Kim Jong -un, the country has not given the people anything," he said. Young people now question what the country has given them.

Zhiyan said that in order to implement this law, the government has established a group and "relentlessly" fights everywhere to fight anything that is considered anti -socialism. "People don't trust each other now, and the fear is huge."

Zhiyan said she was taken to ask for this new law. Since she was questioned, she no longer revealed her true thoughts to others. She is now more afraid of people than before.

For Professor Andreilankov, who has studied North Korea for 40 years, this trust is worrying. "If people don't trust each other, they can't talk about resistance," he said. "This means that North Korea can maintain stability and exist in the next few years or even decades."

In January 2023, the government passed another law to prohibit people from using vocabulary reminiscent of Korean dialects. Violation of this law may also constitute a death penalty in the most extreme circumstances. Zhiyan said that the law is now too much to remember, and those who are taken away may not know which one they have been accused. If they want to ask, the prosecutor will only answer, "You don't need to know which law you have committed."

"The three Korean people who interviewed the interviews confirmed a amazing point of view. North Korea is more high and totalitarian than in the past at any time." Korea's Sokeel Park said, "This is the disaster tragedy that is currently being performed."

Recently, there are signs that the authorities may be open to the border. Ming Shu and Chanhao, who lived near the border, said that most of them in the town had vaccinated the new crown vaccine -they estimated that it was a Chinese vaccine -in Pyongyang, Zhiyan said that a considerable number of people had already vaccinated two shots Essence In addition, customs data shows that the country is allowing some grains and flour to be imported from China again, which is likely to be to alleviate the shortage and avoid famine that many people are afraid of.

The control system that appears during the popular period is likely to be consolidated. This will make it more difficult for us to understand this country, and it is a pity that it will be much more difficult to understand everything that happens to what they have been instilled. "They must participate in the life summary every week, which is the mandatory activity of each citizen. Here, they have to admit their mistakes and failures while reporting their shortcomings. These meetings are designed to encourage good behavior and take out unusual molecules. They can never admit it in the classroom, but Chanhao said that people no longer believe in the publicity on TV.

"The country tells us that we are inhabited in the arms of our mother, but what kind of mother will kill him because the child does not want to starve in China because the child does not want to hungry?" He asked. "Before the new crown, people's views on Kim Jong -un are positive," Ming Shu said. "But now, almost everyone is dissatisfied."

Zhiyan remembers that when Kim Jong -un and US President Trump met with nuclear weapons in 2018, she was full of hope and joy, thinking that maybe she could go to foreign travel soon. The negotiations have been ruptured later. Since then, Kim Jong -un has continued to use its limited finances for nuclear weapons development and reject all diplomatic proposals in the international community. In 2022, he conducted a record number of missile tests.

"We were deceived," Zhiyan said, "Border blockade made our lives back 20 years. We feel deeply betrayed."

"The people never want this endless weapon development, it brings hardships to generations," she sighed.

Chanhao accused the international community. "The United States and the United Nations seem to be stupid," he said, questioning why they still proposed to negotiate with Kim Jong -un, it is clear that he would not give up nuclear weapons. On the contrary, the construction worker also hopes that the United States will attack his country.

"We can live only through war and get rid of the entire leadership," he said. "We must end this regime in some ways."

Ming Shu agreed to this. "If you start war, people will abandon our government," she said, "This is reality."

But Yan Yan hopes to have a simple way. She wants to live in a society where people are not hungry, neighbors can live, and they do not need to monitor each other. They can eat rice in three meals a day.

When we heard her news last time, she did not have enough food to feed the child.

We submit our survey results to the Korean government. The representative of the country's embassy in London said: "The information you collected is not exactly in line with the facts, because it is a testimony from the forces of the Anti -North Korea's Democratic People's Republic. One, and unswervingly maintain the well -being of the people. "

"Even in the face of the test and challenge, the people's well -being is our first priority."

This agreement stipulates that Sino -US scientists will cooperate in basic research in the fields of atmosphere, agriculture, physics, and chemistry

(Voice of Germany) more than 40 years ago, on January 31, 1979, when the leader of the Chinese Communist Party Deng Xiaoping visited the United States, he signed the China -US Science and Technology Cooperation Agreement with then US President Carter when he visited the United States. This landmark agreement released a strong signal at the time, indicating that even the opponent can still put on the dispute and make common efforts.

At present, the US -China bilateral relations have been in the worst state in the past decades. Several officials familiar with Washington said that the government is postponing the US -China Science and Technology Agreement (STA) as usual later this year.

Although U.S. Secretary of State Brills arrived in Beijing on Sunday for the first time in US Secretary of State's visit to China for the first time, it was basically unwilling to break through the interview. Whether the Sino -US Science and Technology Cooperation Agreement continues the current setbacks, it highlights the following issues: The US government has not yet determined that the benefits of US -China cooperation have more benefits, or are they more risky? This issue is dividing the decision makers of the American politics.

This agreement was signed during the establishment of diplomatic relations between the United States and China. It has been updated every 5 years since then. It has been known as the stable factors in relations between the two countries. The fields of cooperation include basic research in the fields of atmosphere, agriculture, physics, and chemistry. The development of academic and commercial exchanges in the United States and China laid the foundation.

These exchanges have undoubtedly promoted the process of becoming a technology and military power, but at the same time, American politics is concerned about the stolen science and commercial secrets of ChinaSo that the agreement continued before it expired on August 27 this year.

search

salvage

wreckage

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》

Time: 2023-06-18T14:49:38+00:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-18T10:50:99+08:00

Description: Chen Dutian: Compared with the interest rate hike cycle before 2006, the high interest rate environment in this round of high interest rate environment is more pressured on the bank's balance sheet. The perfect soft landing of the Fed needs a little luck.

Images: ["000184779_pic..."]

Themes: ['美联储', '关注']

Keywords: ['美联储', '货币政策', '利率', '美国经济']

Type: Article

The Federal Reserve ’s interest rate interest conference ended on the 14th, and the Monetary Policy Committee decided to maintain interest rates at a range of 5-5.25%. This is the first meeting since the start-up interest rate hike cycle in March 2022. In a policy statement, the Fed stated that "maintaining interest rates unchanged can give the committee the opportunity to evaluate more economic information and its monetary policy meanings in the future." In the summary of economic forecasting, the committee's prediction of economic growth at the end of 2023 has increased. The median number has increased significantly from 0.4%in March to 1%, and the unemployment rate has decreased from 4.5%to 4.1%. 3.6%increased to 3.9%, and the most striking policy interest rates increased from 5.1%to 5.6%.

What are the factors of the three -month interval that has improved the Fed's prediction of the economy? The most important reason may be continuous employment. New non -agricultural employment raised from 217,000 in March to 340,000 in May, exceeding market expectations. In addition, the decline of energy prices and the improvement of the supply chain have also boosted the economy.

Videos: []

Images: ["000000.png"]

The Senate passed this bill with 19 votes on 19 votes. Prime Minister AnthonyalBanese will decide the referendum date within a few weeks. The referendum is currently expected to fall from October to December. This will be the first referendum since Australia held the Republican referendum in 1999. The proposal revised into the Republic system was eventually rejected.

This referendum will become an important moment of politics in Australian countries, which will help define the significance of being Australians and redefine the relationship between Aboriginal people and white people.

If the proposal is passed, the Australian Aboriginal people who have lived in Australia for at least 60,000 years will be recognized for the first time. The Aboriginal people and the Torresstrait islander will also obtain the rights given by the Constitution to give Congress a law that affects their own affairs to the laws that affect their own affairs. Member's suggestions.

Angonis said: "Today, our parliament has said" good "to the referendum. Now, the Australian people will have the opportunity to say" good "to the reconciliation and say" good "to the Aboriginal people to the Constitution.

The polls show that most people support the so -called "Voice of Congress", but as the debate becomes more and more gunpowder, the support rate is also declining.

Australian Aboriginal people account for about 3.2%of the national population of nearly 26 million, and are lower than the national average in most social economic indicators. They used to be marginalized by British colonial rulers and did not obtain voting rights until the 1960s.

How difficult is it to help consumers know palm oil? (Free version)

Authors: ['为环境网站“中外对话”撰稿']

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》

Time: 2023-06-19T00:21:39+00:00

Published Time: 2023-06-18T12:00:99+08:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-18T20:20:99+08:00

Description: Niu and Yu: The sustainability of palm oil has not yet become a public issue in China, but the propaganda activities of private social organizations have initially achieved results, and the instant noodle industry and the cosmetics industry are full of potential.

Images: ["000184785_pic..."]

Themes: ['专栏', '中外对话', '关注']

Keywords: ['中外对话', '橄榄油', '化妆品', '环保', '大宗商品', '马来西亚', '印度尼西亚', '方便面']

Type: Article

Warm reminder from FT Chinese website: If you are interested in the content of more FT Chinese website, please search for "FT Chinese Network" in Apple App Store or Google Application Market and download the official applications of FT Chinese website.

"Do you still remember that you have a habit of looking at the material table recently? Because of your little behavior, you have naturally started to change ..."

At the 15th meeting (COP15) of the Conference of the Contract Council (COP15), which was held in Montreal, Canada in December last year, Wildbound, the non -profit educational organization, released the world's first in the world. Continuous palm oil game- "People in the Forest".

In this text adventure game, players make a choice of consumption, investment and production methods by playing different roles such as ordinary consumers, palm oil companies, and small farmers, so as to produce the habitat and biological diversity of red hair orangutan Different effects.

In recent years, Chinese folk social organizations have carried out many activities to increase the awareness of palm oil of Chinese consumers. Palm oil has not yet become a public issue in China. Most Chinese people know nothing about palm oil, let alone care about its sustainable issues. Ru Mingyi, the chief Development Officer of Ye Sheng, said, "It is a long -term job to improve the awareness of Chinese consumers' palm oil. Although it is full of challenges, it is by no means impossible."

According to the "2022 Sustainable Consumption Report" jointly released by Shangdao and interface news, with the publicity of the government's "double carbon" goals, more and more Chinese consumers recognize the impact of their consumer behavior on the environment and society. As the main consumer population, consumers aged 21-140 are more likely to be guided by low -carbon information. Not only can they accept higher premiums, they are also willing to share their experiences. However, the report also mentioned that the popularity of most sustainable relevant certification standards and logos remains to be improved, and sustainable palm oil is one of them.

Palm oil for consumer invisible palm oil

China is the world's second largest palm oil importer and the third largest consumer country. In the past two years (2020 and 2021), China's palm oil imports have remained at about 7 million tons, mainly from Indonesia and Malaysia.

Although China has high demand for palm oil, its demand for sustainable palm oil is very low. According to a 2020 report from the United Nations Development Program, only about 1%of the palm oil imported from China have obtained sustainable certification. Similarly, a study by the World Natural Foundation (WWF) in 2021 shows that only about 4-7%of Chinese consumed palm oil has passed the Roundtableon Sustainable Palm Oil (RSPO) certification.

Insufficient consumer awareness is one of the reasons for China's limited demand for sustainable palm oil. 80%of China's imported palm oil is applied to the food industry, but most Chinese consumers do not know the palm oil that eats into the belly. The Consumer Survey conducted by the Beijing Representative Office of the World Nature Foundation showed that 46%of the 5,000 respondents had not heard of palm oil, let alone the connection between unsustainable palm oil and forest cutting.

The reason for this phenomenon is that the fuzzy label makes the palm oil be invisible in the consumer market. Since 2014, EU laws have demanded the specific types of vegetable oils (including palm oil) on the food component table. Under the requirements of the current bills in China and many other countries, foods using palm oil only need to mark "vegetable oil" on the packaging. In addition, the palm oil industry produces many complex derivatives for home supplies and personal care products. These products usually do not clearly indicate that palm oil is the original ingredient, and users naturally cannot know.

The discussion of palm oil about palm oil is not much, and what initially attracted attention was its impact on health. In 2005, a instant noodle brand played the slogan "Non -Fried" in the advertisement, and the palm oil used by fried instant noodles also entered the consumer's vision. However, the public's attention to palm oil was once limited to whether the characteristics of the high saturated fat content brought health risks. People's Health Network posted that "Although too much intake is not good for health, the human body also needs an appropriate amount of saturated fatty acids. "" ".

How to make palm oil be seen?

The low awareness of palm oil for ordinary public has increased difficulty to consumers' propaganda and advocacy activities. Lu Mingyi introduced that in order to attract more people to participate, the current domestic activities are generally designed and promoted and educated projects under the framework of biological diversity and forest protection.

In 2020, RSPO and Wild Sheng cooperated to launch the "Changemakers for Nature" initiative. Co -founder Isabelnepstad and Yao Songqiao initially hoped to bring young people to Amazon Rainforest, witness the cutting forests of the cut, and intuitively experience the importance of protecting forests and biological diversity.

Due to the epidemic, the goal becomes difficult to implement, and the participants can only learn through online and offline courses, and create their own influence items and solutions after the course. The content of the course also includes the knowledge of sustainable palm oil. One of the trainees Yang Yang produced a sustainable palm oil initiative short film "Behind the Shelves", and the entire platform played more than one million times.

Lu Mingyi said that the biggest difficulty encountered in the process is that it is difficult to buy products with sustainable palm oil certification in the market. Therefore, this concept can only be implemented when organizing activities, and there is no corresponding product and consumption scenario to match. Even if consumers agree with the importance of sustainable palm oil, it is difficult to make practical changes when buying.

Natural founders have tried to advocate the production of some sustainable products. However, companies have found that the entire procurement process of sustainable palm oil is more complicated, long cycles and not flexible. "So simple. In the end, they lost their interest, and they were only willing to wait until the industrial chain was relatively sound before trying.

In addition to educating young consumers, they also chose to cooperate with Nanjing Hongshan Zoo to integrate the relevant information of sustainable palm oil into the "Orangutan Care Week Tour Club" held by the zoo and promote tourists. Lu Mingyi believes that after visiting the red -haired orangutan in the zoo, he associated with them, and it was more effective to advocate on this basis.

The Linzhong game game introduced at the beginning of the article also started with the protection of red Moso Orangutan and promoted the importance of sustainable palm oil on the protection of red orangutan and its habitat, but the internal logic was also directly linked to the supply chain of palm oil.

Can companies guide consumers?

The certified sustainable palm oil will generate a premium of 3%-30%. If consumers have a low awareness of sustainable palm oil and they are unwilling to pay for the premium. Willing to invest in sustainable authentication products.

However, the CDP Global Environmental Information Research Center's interview with Chinese companies in 2020 shows that companies are increasingly aware of the potential long -term costs of unsustainable palm oil on the environmental impact of supply chain elasticity.In addition, as consumers' sustainable awareness increases, it is recognized that the negative impact of the unsustainable palm oil purchased by the company on the environment will constitute risks on the company's reputation. If more and more companies can realize such long -term costs and change the mentality of avoiding risks, it will help the development of sustainable palm oil.

Fang Lifeng, the person in charge of RSPO China, said that the main work of RSPO in China is to further enhance the industry's awareness and awareness and cognition of sustainable palm oil, and mobilize more companies to purchase sustainable palm oil. At present, there are more than 300 Chinese members. If some leading companies are willing to propagate and guide consumers while purchasing sustainable palm oil, consumer consciousness will gradually increase, and it will also stimulate other companies in the industry to purchase sustainable products.

Promoting sustainable palm oil in the instant noodles and the cosmetics industry

One quarter of the palm oil imported from China is used for instant noodles, and currently more than 70%of the world's individual protection and cosmetics products contain one or more palm oil derivatives. Starting from these two industries, it has promoted the certified sustainable palm oil to Chinese consumers to increase consumer awareness and has more potential.

Master Kong, who occupied nearly half of China's market share, wrote in the 2022 Sustainable Development Annual Report, "We are committed to reducing the negative impact of packaging and palm oil procurement on the forest. Certification. The statement may be misleading. Master Kang is not a member of RSPO. The proportion of suppliers obtained by RSPO certification does not mean that its procurement certification palm oil ratio.

According to the report of Palm Oil in WWF2022, the relevant costs of corporate transitions to sustainable palm oil and certification agencies include membership, evaluation, audit, documents, training, and premiums for certified palm oil. The report estimates that the average of 70 grams of instant noodles per pack, the cost burden brought by the enterprise is 0.0009 US dollars, which can be ignored.

Fang Lifeng introduced that the premium exists objectively. In particular, it is convenient for palm oil, with limited gross profit in the industry and fierce competition among enterprises. But this does not mean that the industry has no room for transformation. Some Japanese instant noodle companies have promised to use 100%sustainable palm oil. In the end, it is still depending on the company's willingness to move and long -term business goals.

In contrast, cosmetics consumers have a high ability to withstand premiums. Investigators of WWF 2018 also showed that consumers generally accepted sustainable palm oil (especially cosmetics and personal care products) premiums were 6%to 10%. Under the trend of sustainable cosmetics, the makeup protection industry has also become a potential breakthrough to increase consumers' awareness of sustainable palm oil.

In recent years, sustainable cosmetics have set off a trend in China. In 2021, Tmall International defined the "Cleanbeauty" for the first time, including palm oil that does not use non -RSPO certification. After the concept was proposed, many consumers were sought after by the "pure beauty" brand of environmentally friendly environment. The sales of this category increased by more than 600%year-on-year sales in January-June.

In 2021, RSPO delivered a speech at the International Cosmetics Innovation Conference in Shanghai as a special guest. It is mainly determined by the raw material of the product. The sustainability of the ingredients in the product formula is also the main consideration. "

Fang Lifeng also observed that, as an important component of beauty care products, the awareness of the beauty industry has gradually increased the awareness of sustainable palm oil, and the relevant parties of the industry's interests are becoming more and more willing to discuss this issue.

From the perspective of the industry, China's local brands are relatively late, and international beauty brands occupy most of the market. In 2021, French personal care company L'Oreal's share in the Chinese cosmetics market was about 12.2%, ranking first, and L'Oreal's palm oil had passed RSPO certification 100%.

"International brands make commitments and promote the implementation of China's supply chain in the Chinese market, so that many local Chinese companies realize that if they do not take measures and purchase sustainable palm oil, corporate reputation will face additional risks. In China, it also exists in the world. At the same time, large enterprises can move first, which can strengthen the capacity building of domestic sustainable palm oil suppliers, but also increase consumer awareness in publicity, "said Fang Lifeng.

China and the United States have bilateral talks in Beijing on Sunday. The picture shows the US delegation

I hope that the United States will adhere to the objective and rational cognition of China and do it with China to maintain Sino -US relations well to maintain Sino -US relations. Political foundation, calm, professional, and rational handling accidental occasional incidents.

The Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs stated that the two sides should fall into the consensus of the internship and Biden in Bali to promote the stability of Sino -US relations and return to the right track. The two sides also agreed to continue to promote the Sino -US joint work group to solve specific problems in Sino -US relations.

The statement also said that both parties agreed to encourage the expansion of humanities and educational exchanges between the two countriesIn order to increase passenger flights between China and the United States, the two sides welcomed more students, scholars, and business people to visit each other, and provided support and convenience for this. Qin Gang also clarified the US's core interests and major concerns on the core interests and major concerns of the Taiwan issue, and made a clear position to the United States, and made clear requirements for the United States.

Qin Gang pointed out that the issue of Taiwan is the core of China's core interests, the most significant issue of Sino -US relations, and the most prominent risk. China urges the United States to abide by the three joint communiqués of China and China and the United States. Fall to practice.

US State Department spokesman Matthewmiller also issued a statement on Sunday saying that Brinken held a frank, substantial and constructive talks with Qin Gang in Beijing. Brinken emphasizes the importance of diplomacy between the two countries and maintains open communication channels on all issues to reduce the risk of misunderstanding and misjudgment.

The United States stated that Brinson raised some concern issues in the meeting and proposed the opportunity to explore cooperation with China on a common multinational issue with China under the same interest. The United States will always defend the interests and values of the American people, and cooperate with its allies and partners to promote the United States' vision of a world of free, openness and maintaining international rules -based order. Qin Gang pointed out the importance of promoting the exchanges of the United States and China.

However, a report by Politico, a politician website, believes that Brins are ambiguous and indicate that his agenda project has hardly achieved substantial progress 。

Sino -US relations to thaw?

The Associated Press reported that this talk may pave the way for Biden and Xi Jinping's meeting in the next few months.

Biden said on Saturday (17th) that he hoped to meet Xi Jinping in the next few months to solve too much differences that caused them.

However, the United States and China failed to overcome the most serious differences during the bilateral foreign ministers talks, but they could discuss these differences in potential constructive ways and agree to continue negotiations. Neither sides showed any tendency to abandon their established position.

This long negotiation list includes various differences from trade to Taiwan, the human rights situation of China and Hong Kong to the military in China in the South China Sea, and various differences in the Russian and Ukraine War.

During Sunday talks, Blint also urged China to release the detained U.S. citizens and take measures to curb the production and export of fentanyl's raw materials, which helped the American opioid crisis.

(Voice of Germany Chinese website) The Associated Press reported that although various Chinese businesses are "618 Shopping FestivalDuring the period, the price reduction was significantly reduced, attracting billions of dollars to snap -up, but analysts pointed out that the confidence of Chinese consumers is still weak.

From the end of May to June 18th, major Chinese e -commerce companies ushered in the first large -scale shopping festival after clearing the zero. Chinese merchants have sacrificed a large discount, so as to boost sales when the consumption recovery is weaker than expected.

The Chinese official media Xinhua News Agency said that the 618 Shopping Festival is "important nodes that promote consumption potential release" and "testing gold stones that test consumption recovery." It is reported that "the turnover of nearly 50%of small and medium -sized merchants in JD has increased by more than 200%", "Tmall 618 sells for 4 hours, and more than 30 brands of mobile phone digital home appliances have exceeded 100 million yuan." The platform's 618 transcript "witnessed the footsteps of the Chinese consumer market accelerated and recovered."

During the epidemic period last yearNeither Alibaba and JD.com also announced the results of the "Double 11" shopping festival.

The Associated Press quoted analysts that although JD, Tmall, Taobao and PinduoduoWaiting for the shopping platform to provide billions of dollars discounts, the pace of China's consumer market out of the epidemic is still slightly stagnant.

Shaun Rein, the founder of the China Market Research Group (CMR), said that China's consumption confidence is still in a weak state of "geopolitics, weakness after epidemic and domestic politics".

Earlier, the Chinese e -commerce giant "Jingdong" competed with the opponent "Pinduoduo", which is known for its low -cost products, and launched the "10 billion subsidy" plan in March; before, Alibaba's industrial e -commerce group and social e -commerce companies Dai Shan, the president of the business group, also promised that Taobao will "make a huge historic investment in the user size" this year, hoping that merchants can clearly feel that the number of visitors will increase.

Lei Xiaoshan said that under such circumstances, Chinese consumers have been in a state of sensitive prices in the past few months, constantly looking for discounts and price reduction transactions. In the past few years, Chinese merchants have discounted for a long time due to the epidemic. Compared with the previous months, 618 discounts have not been much better, so consumers are unlikely to make more purchases.

According to the Chinese shopping service platform "Buying.com" data, before the epidemic, the total turnover of JD.com's 2019 618 Shopping Festival in 2019 was RMB 2015 billion, and in 2018 it was 159.2 billion. DW tries to check, but many large Chinese media such as Tencent cannot display the web pages of 618 data before the epidemic.

The global economic growth is weak, did our views on globalization wrong?

Creator: PATRICIA COHEN

Publisher: https://www.facebook.com/nytimeschinese

Published Time: 2023-06-19T03:39:45+08:00

Description: The eternal advantage of opening up the market, free trade and efficiency seems to be deviating from the track, and the road to prosperity seems to be becoming darker. It turns out that the surge in economic exchanges between the country and the country failed to bring promise democratic revival. Luis Antonio Rojas for the New York Times Workers of a Chinese company in Mexico. It turns out that China led by the Communist Party is the biggest beneficiary of the global economic system.

Images: ["00econ-rethin..."]

Category: 商业与经济

Type: Article

In 2018, when the global business and political leaders were concentrated in Daalworth to participate in the annual economic forum, the atmosphere was jubilant. The economic growth of all major countries is rising. Knitina Ragard, then president of the International Monetary Fund, declared that the global economy "is in excellent trend"" ".

Five years later, the prospects deteriorated significantly.

"Almost all economic forces that have promoted progress and prosperity over the past 30 years have disappeared," the recently in the World Bank Analysis ReportThe warning said: "The result may be a‘ lost ten years ’ -not just like the past, it happened in some countries or regions -but in the whole world.”

From then on, many things have happened: global epidemic; European war; tension between the United States and China is hot. The inflation, which is considered to be properly preserved like the Disco record collection, has a comeback.

advertise

However, as the dust settled, suddenly, we found that our understanding of the world economy seemed wrong.

Since the collapse of the Berlin Wall more than 30 years ago, the economic agreement that policy makers have rely on -the eternal advantage of open markets, free trade and efficiency -it seems to be deviating from the track.

During the popularity of the new crown virus, the driving force that continued to promote global economic integration and reduced costs caused medical staff NoMask and medical gloves, car manufacturers do not have semiconductors, saw wood factories without wood, and sneakers buyers have no Nike.

At the beginning of 2021, the National Cemetery in New York, when the epidemic was the worst, the number of burials every day was more than doubled. Johnny Milano for the New Yorktimes

In 2020, Bega Momo, Italy, provides care of the new crown patients. When the new crown virus comes, the global reduction of cost and economic integration make it difficult for medical staff to buy masks and other supplies. Fabiobucciarelli for the New York Times

Russian soldiers who invaded Ukraine last year also stepped on the concept of trade and common economic interests to prevent military conflict.

More and more extreme weather destroy cropsForced people to migrate, Make the power plant shutdown, which indicates that the market's invisible hands have not protected the earth.

Today, with the second year of the Ukrainian war, the economic growth of various countries has weak economic growth and continuous inflation.(https://www.foreignaffairs.com/world/why-world-still-needs-trade)[Question] in the field of competition(https://www.brookings.edu/2023/05/02/reactions-to-national-security-advisor-jake-sullivans-brookings-speech/)It became the focus of attention.

advertise

In recent decades, globalization has been regarded as an unstoppable force like gravity, but it is obviously developing in an unpredictable way. The pace of separation of the world economy is accelerating. The best way to deal with it has become a topic of argument.

Of course, the challenge to the dominant economic consensus has been brewing for a long time.

"We see that before the epidemic began, the richest country was frustrated by the Obama government Economic Consultant Committee. It damaged their work and living standards. "

The 2008 financial crisis almost destroyed the global financial system. Britain withdrew from the European Union in 2016. President Trump imposed tariffs on China in 2017, triggering a small trade war.

But starting from the new crown virus, a series of tit -tit -tit -for -comparison crisis has completely exposed the loopholes that need to be concerned.

Just as the consulting company An Yong was in its "2023 Strategic OutlookAs summarized in the summary, the trend behind the growing globalization was "accelerated by the new crowns -and then exacerbated by the Ukrainian war again."

In May, the destroyed Ukraine Bach Murd. Tyler Hicks/The New York Times

This is "the end of history".

Today's anxiety is in sharp contrast to the exciting belief of the exciting victory after the disintegration of the Soviet Union in December 1991. During that period, a theoristIt can be proclaimed that the collapse of communism marks "the end of history"——Shaxual and democratic thought not only defeated the opponent, but also represented" the end of the evolution of human ideology ".

advertise

The relevant economic theories of global free market capitalism have also covered similar luster, as if it is impossible to defeat and inevitably. Open markets, non -interference governments, and unremitting pursuit of efficiency will provide the best way to prosper.

It is believed that the new world of goods, money, and information in the world's crisscrossing will basically eliminate the old order of the Cold War conflict and the non -democratic regime.

People have reason to feel optimistic. In the 1990s, the inflation rate was very low, and the employment rate, salary and productivity were rising. Global trade almost turned over. Investment in developing countries surge. The stock market rises.

The World Trade Organization was established in 1995 to perform these rules. Six years later, the joining of China is deemed to have changed significance. Establishing a huge market with 142 countries will inevitably lead the Asian giant to democracy.

Together with China, South Korea, Malaysia and other countries, China has turned the difficult farmers into a productive forces of urban factory workers. Furniture, toys and electronic products they sell around the world have brought huge growth.

China joined the signature ceremony of the World Trade Organization in 2001. Reuters

This people's love of the economic route has helped create amazing wealth, causing hundreds of millions of people to get rid of poverty and promote amazing technological progress.

But there are shocking failures. Globalization has accelerated climate change and deepened inequality.

advertise

In the United States and other developed economies, many industrial workers' positions have been exported to countries with lower wages, and people have lost a springboard to the middle class.

Policy makers have always knew that there will always be winners and losers. People who hope.

Regardless of the protection of workers, environmental impacts or democratic rights, companies have begun to find low -paying workers worldwide. They found many such people in Mexico, Vietnam and China.

TV, T -shirts and corn cakes are cheaper than ever, but many necessities such as medical care, housing and higher education are getting out of reach.

Employment outflow has lowered domestic wages, weakened the bargaining ability of workers, stimulated anti -immigrant emotions, and strengthened the U.S. Donald Trump, Hungarian Olban Victor, and Maline Le Pen in France. Leader's status.

In developed industrial countries such as the United States, the United Kingdom, and several European countries, political leaders cannot or are unwilling to re -assign returns and burdens.

advertise

They also have no ability to stop destructive environmental impactEssence The transportation of goods in the world has increased greenhouse gas emissions. Consumption of consumers around the world has made natural resources nervous, which has encouraged excessive fishing in Southeast Asia and illegal cutting forests in Brazil. Cheap production facilities pollute countries with appropriate environmental standards.

It turns out that the market itself cannot automatically allocate income and cannot stimulate developing countries to develop or establish a democratic system.

US National Security Consultant Jack Shalvin in Recent SpeechAccording to China, a core fallacy of the US economic policy is to assume that "no matter what our competitors do, no matter how much the challenges we face, no matter how many guardrails we dismantle, the market can always effectively allocate capital."

The surge in economic exchanges between the country and the country has failed to bring promise democracy.

It turns out that China under the leadership of the Communist Party is the biggest beneficiary of the global economic system -perhaps the master of this system -but not embracing democratic values.

"Capitalism tools are in the hands of socialists," said Deng Xiaoping, a Chinese leader in 1992. At that time, China was developing into a world factory. China's amazing growth has made it the main engine of the world's second largest economy and global growth. However, Beijing has always maintained strict control over raw materials, land, capital, energy, credit and labor, as well as the people's actions and remarks.

Globalization has a huge impact on the environment, including forests in the Malaysia, Brazil's Malaysia. Victor Moriyama for the New York Times

Food was distributed in Johannesburg in 2020, which caused a significant increase in the demand for assistance. JOAO SILVA/The New York Times

The funds are here, and the poor country pays the price.

In developing countries, the results may be bad.

The economic destruction caused by the major epidemic, coupled with the soaring food and fuel prices caused by the Ukrainian war, triggered a series of debt crisis. Rising interest rates make these crises more serious. Like energy and food, debt is usually denominated in the world market, so when the US interest rate rises, debt payments become more expensive.Poor countries have been forced to completely cancel the restrictions of capital entering and leaving the country. The reason for this is that funds should be freely flowing between the country like commodities. The government, enterprises, and individuals borrow money from foreign lenders will provide funds for industrial development and key infrastructure.

"Financial globalization should have brought developing countries into an era of strong growth and fiscal stability," said Jiadi Gosh, an economist at the University of Massachusetts Amhaster. But "the result is counterproductive."

Some loans -whether it is from private lenders or institutions from the World Bank -none of them have sufficient returns to repay debts. There are also some loans that have been put into speculative projects, incomplete proposals, face engineering, or entering the bank account of corrupt officials. The debt country is still around the interest rate, and the rise in interest rates will instantly increase the scale of debt payment.

Over the years, the poor loans, asset bubbles, currency fluctuations and official management have led to the cycle of prosperity and depression in Asia, Russia, Latin America and other places. In Sri LankaThe luxury project from the port to the boarding courts initiated by the government has led to the country's bankruptcy last year, and the citizens were looking for food. The central bank paid Iranian oil in the form of earthenware transactions to pay Iranian oil.

This is a "Ponzi scam", Gosh said.

The private lenders were worried that the debt country could not repay, and suddenly cut off the flow of funds, causing these countries to be in trouble.

International Monetary Fund(IMF)With compulsory tightening policies, the bailout is forced to cut over -expanded government cuts. It usually leads to many people suffering by cutting public assistance, pensions, education and medical care.

Even IMF economists are in 2016 AcknowledgeInstead, such policies have not brought growth, but "exacerbated inequality, and endangered long -lasting development."

The disappointment of the Western loan method gives China the opportunity to loans from countries such as Argentina, Mongolia, Egypt, and Surinan.

A market in Buenos Aires. China is actively lending in Argentina and other countries. Sarah Pabst for the New York Times

Self -sufficient self -sufficient replacement of cheap imports.

Although the disintegration of the Soviet Union has cleared the road for the orthodox free market, the Russian Federation's invasion of Ukraine has now decisively leaving this road.

Professor of Henry Farrell, Professor of Senior International Research Institute of Johns Hopkins University(https://sais.jhu.edu/users/hfarrel1)Said that today's international economy can outline "how geopolitics devour super globalization."

The politics of the old world style has subverted the assumptions of the global economic order -this is the threat of the catastrophic climate collapse, the fierce social turmoil and the increasing inequality of inequality.

Leader of EU Foreign Affairs and Security Policy Hessep BorielIn an invasion of Ukraine for 10 months, it bluntly stated: "We have decomposed the source of prosperity with the source of security." Europe has obtained cheap energy from Russia, and has obtained cheap finished products from China. "That world no longer exists," he said.

The bottleneck of supply chain caused by the popular and subsequent recovery has highlighted the vulnerability of the global procurement economy. As the political tensions caused by war intensified, policy makers quickly added self -sufficiency and strength to the goals of growth and efficiency.

"Our supply chain UnsafeThere is no elasticity, "the Minister of Finance Jennite L. Yellen said last spring. She said that the establishment of trade relations should focus on" trustworthy partners ", even if this means that" the cost level is slightly higher, the system efficiency is slightly lower, the less system efficiency is slightly lower "" ".

"It is too naive to think that the market is about efficiency and power without power," Abraham Newman said that he co -authored "Underground Empire: How the United States has weapons the world economy"(Underground Empire: How America Weaponized the World Economy)This book.

The nature of the economic network determines that it can cause imbalance and pressure on power, because the abilities, resources and weaknesses of various countries are different.

Russia provides 40%of the EU's natural gas, which tries to use the EU's dependence to pressure it and require it to withdraw its support for Ukraine.

The United States and its allies use their dominant positions for the global financial system to remove major Russian banks from the international payment system.

Jonorosk, near Oeda last year. In 2021, Ukraine is the world's largest wheat exporter. Laetitia vancon for the new Yorktimes

Grapes are harvested in a vineyard in South Australia. After Australia expressed its support for Taiwan, China issued an import ban on wine and other products in the country. Adam Ferguson for thenew York Times

China restricts trading partners into its huge market for revenge.

The extreme concentration of key suppliers and information technology networks have produced more bottlenecks.

China has manufactured 80%of the world's solar panels. Taiwan produces 92%of micro -advanced semiconductors. Most of the world's trade and transactions are calculated in US dollars.

The new reality is reflected in the US policy. The United States -the main founder of the Liberalization Economic Order and the World Trade Organization, the more comprehensive free trade agreement, and repeatedly refused to comply with the decision of the WTO.It also adopts Chinese -style industrial policies to provide huge subsidies for electric vehicles, batteries, wind farms, solar power plants, etc. to ensure the security of the supply chain and speed up the transition to renewable energy.

"The economic dependence, which has been established for decades, has become very dangerous." Said Sausa, a national security consultant. He also said that it was wrong to persist in "too simplified market efficiency".

Although the previous economic orthodox has been partially abandoned, it is unclear what it will be replaced. The current mainstream approach is improvisationEssence Maybe the only assumption that must be reliable now is that the road to prosperity and policy weighing will become even more unclear.

A solar power field in China. This country produces 80%of the world's solar panels. Gilles Sabrié for the New York Times

Li Qiang visited Germany, where is Sino -German relations going?

Creator: ERIKA SOLOMON,NICOLE HONG

Publisher: https://www.facebook.com/nytimeschinese

Published Time: 2023-06-19T05:33:54+08:00

Description: The two countries restarted government consultations after the epidemic. However, in the case of increasingly tight relations between the Ukrainian war and Sino -US relations, Germany wanted to maintain a necessary economic connection with Beijing and security concerns. How the two sides adjust the relationship and face challenges. Markus Schreiber/Associated Press last week, German Chancellor Tsubitz introduced a new security strategy in Germany at a press conference in Berlin.

Images: ["19germany-chi...", "19germany-chi..."]

Category: 中国

Type: Article

Berlin -Ten years ago, when China and Germany began to conduct government consultations, Angra Merkel was still the Prime Minister, and relations between the two countries seemed to mean endless trade and profit opportunities. During the dialogue period, there was unprecedented prosperity, with trade agreements and signature ceremonies, and red carpets and military ceremonies.

But on Tuesday, after the three -year interruption of the epidemic, German Chancellor Olaf Tumolz and Chinese Prime Minister Li Qiang will be in a very different world -a world that has new considerations on political fragility and economic dependence -re -re -considered Start consultation.

The two countries have returned to talks with almost alienated partners. Their relationship became nervous due to the deepening of Russia's war in Ukraine, the deepening of the friendly relations between Beijing and Moscow, and the tension between China and Germany's most important allies in the United States.

"These consultations seem to be not synchronized with the times," said Tolstine Benner, director of the Berlin Global Public Policy Research Institute. "Affairs between governments is usually what you and your democratic allies will do. The challenge we face is to get a balance between the new realism we face and the Merkel -style consultation with China."

This month, the 28th mechanized brigade of Ukraine, which was deployed in the south of Bachurut, started fire at the Russian position and was taken this month. Tyler Hicks/The New York Times

This will be the first consultation of Shuoerz, and Li Qiang is also the first visit to Berlin as the Prime Minister. It will accompany him to visit a large number of ministers. There is no doubt that their tasks will conflict, even if they try to shape the areas of common interests.

For Germany, this meeting will be an opportunity to declare a new position, that is, China is still one of its most important economic partners, but it is also a "systemic competitor." This means that Berlin will try to protect its key technologies and encourage their companies to stay away from Beijing and achieve diversification.

For China, this will be a greatest European trading partner to persist in all opportunities -and make a gap between Berlin and Washington.

Today, the pressure from the United States to fight against Germany to fight against Beijing is increasing. How to maintain the necessary economic connection with China under such shadows is a balance between Germany is still working hard.

A German official said that it was a "three -body problem" in Berlin. German officials are keenly aware that Washington is a security guarantee, and they can no longer expect to treat economic interests separately from political interests.

Germany once regarded Germany, China, Germany and the United States, and the United States and China as each other's independent bilateral relations, but now they feel that they are tangled together. Safety concerns also interfered with Germany's economic ambitions in unprecedented ways.

Russia's invasion of Ukraine Forced Germany to re -consider its economic relationship that it had been regarded as naturalFor example, Russia once provided 50%of natural gas supply to Germany. Germany managed to turn to other energy supply, barely avoided a serious energy crisis, although it was not avoided to avoid economic recession.

Baltic Sea, Germany City Rubbing Outdoor Beixi No. 2 pipeline. Lena Mucha for the New York Times

In contrast, incidents such as China attacking Taiwan have caused Sino -US military confrontation to be much more painful. German officials believe that they will now be forced to be involved in it. Previously, they once vigorously promoted Asian countries to support Europe to oppose Russia's invasion of Ukraine, thinking that this was an act of violating territorial sovereignty.

Economic consequences will be more serious: more than 1 million German jobsRelying on China directly, there are more positions indirectly relying on China. In Europe's investment in ChinaMen, nearly halfFrom Germany, nearly halfPart of the supply chain of German manufacturing companies depends on China.

advertise

This is also a difficult time for China.

After the popularity, China's economic recovery speed is slower than expected. Some Western companies are also cautious about making new investment in China, because President Xi Jinping has begun to promote strengthening national security this year -including expanding anti -spy law and strengthening police's review of Western companies in China.

Sino -German relations are particularly important: it is the source of China's largest European trading partners and the source of European foreign investment.

Hu Chunchun, an associate professor of Shanghai University of Foreign Languages, said: "Germany has been talking about reducing risks or reducing dependence on the Chinese market. This fact naturally makes China worry."

In May, Chinese Prime Minister Li Qiang met with Russian Prime Minister Mikhail Mashass in Beijing. POOL Photo by Thomas Peter-POOL

In Berlin talks, German officials are likely to let China understand the content of Chinese strategic documents they have never announced. As the German government's position around its position should last for several months, the document is postponed. It is expected to be announced in July.advertise

Under the pressure of Tsumers, the tone of the document is expected to soften because he is worried that it will have a great impact on the economy that has fallen into a decline.

German officials will make it clear that they have no intention of changing the "one China" policy, while recognizing the goal of Beijing unified Taiwan, while maintaining a "friendly but unofficial" relationship with Taiwan.

They will also emphasize a message conveyed many times: Germany does not have a plan to "decompose" with China, as U.S. officials have urged. But on the contrary, it tends to the concept of "risk".

Analysts said the question is how to define the true meaning of "de -risk".

"Does this mean to remove risks, or minimize the risk? Do you want to do this at a fast speed? There is a big room for this statement," Benner said. "Tsold is careful. He is doing the" de -risk "of the lightweight version. He pays great attention to decentralizing risks, but he does not want to hinder investment."

In April, China had lifted a strict epidemic restriction measures, a shopping area in Beijing. Kevin Frayer/Getty Images

In April of this year, some news reports that Berlin is considering restricting the sale of chemicals for semiconductors in Beijing, and Chinese officials are concerned about Germany. The United States has been seeking support from Europe and other allies to prevent China from obtaining key technologies such as semiconductors, which has furious China.

"They need to keep the Europeans stay away from Americans as much as possible," Hu Yongkong, Executive Director of the Institute of Merkato China Research Institute(Mikkohuotari)When talking about the goal of the Chinese delegation's visit to Germany this week. "In this regard, Germany plays a huge role."

advertise

Han Lei's(Paul Haenle)It is said that the Beijing side still hopes to be in such a fact that many European companies are seriously dependent on Chinese consumers, and they cannot bear the cost of maintaining a distance from China.

He said: "The abacus of Chinese leaders is that Europe still play a large extent."

Especially for Germany, China has cards to play: run counter to many more vigilant German companies. Chemical producers BASF and Volkswagen's largest and most powerful companies such as Volkswagen and other automotive manufacturers have increased their investment in China.

At the end of last year, China had canceled strict epidemic restrictions, reopening the economy, and at the same time spread the red carpet to encourage foreign investors to invest in China. Volkswagen's CEO Oliver Brumer is one of the first batch of leaders of multinational enterprises visiting China. China is the largest market for the car manufacturer.

"China thinks that due to the dependence of a small number of major German companies, Germany will always compromise, or at least reached an agreement with China," Luke(Philippele correct)explain.

In fact, the biggest challenge facing Germany may not be a showdown with China, but to be with their own companies -to indicate that they must rely on China to continue their own risks in the future.

What is the new China -German government consultation? (Free version)

Authors: ['为FT中文网撰稿']

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》
