On June 19, Li Qiang, the State Council of the Chinese State Council, visited Europe, conducted a formal visit to Germany and participated in seven rounds of China -German government consultations. French official visit and attended the new global financing contract summit. This is the first visit after Li Qiang took office, which fully reflects the high attention of China ’s China -Europe relations. After all, Europe is always the object of China to fight against the United States to try to win, and the leadership of Germany and France in Europe has become the target of China to strive for.

During his visit to Germany, the Sino -German government will hold a new round of government consultations. As the first consultation between the new government between the two sides, the economic community and the media of the two countries have paid great attention to the government consultations in this round. In addition, Li Qiang will also attend the 11th Sino -German Economic and Technological Cooperation Forum and conduct in -depth exchanges with representatives of the two economic circles.

Although it is not yet possible to guess whether both and Germany will eventually reach some consensus, from the perspective of results, it will definitely be much "restrained" than in the past. After all, for the German side, it is too high -profile. G7 member states explain. Regardless of the results, this round of consultations should be tentatively tone for Sino -German future politics and economic and trade toward. Once the direction is determined, even if the external environment is changing at all times, the essence of Sino -German relations in the future will not have much guessing space. Just as the German "China Strategy", for this dragging report, all walks of life does not seem to make much expectations. After all, when the German government is regarded as "competitors" and "institutional opponents", "China "Strategy" The rest of the focus may be on wording and tone.

"Preheating" "Preheating" **

Originally, the Beijing Representative Office of the German Industry and Commerce Conference and the German Chamber of Commerce planned to host a "Sino -German -level high -level government -enterprise dialogue" event on June 8. This event invited Roberthabeck, Deputy Prime Minister of Germany and Minister of Economic and Climate Protection, Dr. Frank Ruekert, the German Minister of Germany, Peter Adrian, Chairman of the German Industry and Commerce Conference, and Hubertustroska, Chairman of the German Chamber of Commerce. It is regarded by the outside world as a warm -up of the China -German government consultation in this round. The enthusiastic registration of German companies seems to herald the German economic circles' desire to find out the direction of the German Germany. However, good things are worn more. The week before the event, the organizer announced that the event would be postponed.

In order to support this "warm -up activity of the German government consultation", the German Chamber of Commerce in China also did a small fast survey (FlashSurvey) in mid -May and planned "Dialogue" announced the relevant results before the abroad. It was thought that the preheating preheating will be canceled with the postponement of the big activity, but it arrives as scheduled, but the result is not as optimistic as expected.

This Flashsurvey is a survey on business confidence in all member companies after the results of the German business business survey at the end of last year after the results of the business confidence survey of Germany's business at the end of last year. Later business emotions, but due to consumer consumption and geopolitical tension, the business confidence of Waldes' enterprises was still sluggish in the post -epidemic period.

Survey results show:

• The business prospects of the Wald Enterprise are half -mixed: Although China's "zero -zero policy" has ended, 22%of companies are still expected to remain unchanged in the development of its industry in 2023; even one -third (even one -third ( 35%) Enterprises are expected to worsen the development of the industry; but more than 40%(43%) companies say they will improve.

• Both turnover and profit growth are lower than expected: the number of companies with a decline in turnover and profit declines have nine and ten percentage points than in 2022.

• The end of the Qing Zero policy did not boost investment confidence: 55%of German companies plan to increase investment in China in the next two years, which is four percentage points from the results of 2022, but far lower than the level of previous years (2019: 67 %, 2020: 72%, 2021: 71%)

• Market development is lower than expected and geopolitical factors hinders investment, but competition promotes investment: The main reasons for companies that do not invest in enterprises come from low expectations of market growth, continuous geopolitical tensions, and China's independent controlled policies; in increasing investment in investment; Enterprises: 62%of companies will continue to invest in maintaining their competitiveness in the Chinese market. 48%of companies are expected to benefit from market growth potential.

• The trend of localization and diversification continues: The strategy of the corporate headquarters responding to the intensified situation of geopolitical tensions includes expanding the diversified development of the region outside China and the degree of localization in China.

(Appendent complete Research Results.

Localization, diversification

As mentioned in the article that I commented on the article of Tsutz's visit to China last year, the German energy crisis caused by the Russian and Ukraine War caused the German government to reflect, and there was a huge hidden danger to an excessive dependence on a entity. Such hidden dangers today are the energy crisis caused by too dependence on Russia. Tomorrow may be the supply chain crisis (such as rare earth) caused by excessive dependence on China. This also prompted the German government for safety and hedging considerations to prepare early for possible extreme conditions.

But if it is just to avoid danger, the starting point of Germany's strategy to China is different from the United States. Therefore, the "decoupling" theory between China and the United States is not suitable for plagiarism in Germany (and even Europe), not to mention that German companies have also expressed their conflict with "decoupling". Therefore, when the European Union Commission chairman Feng Delin made a speech on the European Union's Chinese policy, "de-Risking" became the main tone of the Western camp strategy to China.

"Risk" is the existence of risk. But it may not be so simple to eliminate the German's determination of risks. Fortunately, the German government's "risk" of the German government may not buy it. Because regardless of whether the "risk" is to reduce the existing dependence or reduce future dependence, just from the perspective of the consumer market scale, labor quality, raw material supply stability, and industrial chain integrity, if you want to find one in a short period of time The single market completely replaces China, and it is really unlikely that at best it is a "flat replacement". "Localization" and "diversification" have also become two variables, allowing German companies to adjust their own strategies to China by their own proportion in the global market. Increased, stock

In 45 years of reform and opening up, China has experienced a series of transformations from scratch to upgrading, and also has a huge domestic demand market. After joining the WTO in 2001 Giant international market. The superposition of the two incremental markets outside and inside has made enterprises get used to "adding additions" in the process of high -speed development. However, with the continuous rise in raw material costs, labor costs, and operating costs, the advantages of Chinese manufacturing have weakened. Coupled with the weakness of the domestic demand market, the transformation of consumption and investment awareness caused by the epidemic, the Sino -US trade friction and the Russian and Ukraine conflict The geopolitical impact of geopolitical, the growth rate of the incremental market gradually slowed down. When facing the "subtraction", companies that are used to "adding additions" will perform more "volume", especially in the stock market.

In order to get more stock market share or ensure that the existing share is not divided, on the one hand, the Walted Enterprise chooses cost reduction and efficiency, and actively enhances competitiveness to meet the localization needs of customers. On the other hand, on the other hand, It is also actively seeking the support of the Chinese government: calling on the government to stimulate consumption, boost confidence, call on the Chinese government to increase the openness of the market, and provide more fair competition environments.

For the Chinese government, stimulating consumption and boosting confidence is a common demand for interests. However, the latter two points are not so easy. Although the domestic and foreign capital of the Chinese government, such as palms and backs, when the Chinese government's measurement standards for the open market shift from economic benefits to more national security, the natural disadvantages of foreign capital will be prominent. Competition and strengthening the business environment, the palm of the hand is often "inside".

However, this is where the new German government is emphasized. What's more, when the new German government faces China, it will take more pragmatic as a prerequisite for cooperation, and the priority of solving problems will also be higher than the win -win cooperation.

It may be a more effective way to alleviate the game of domestic and foreign capital in the stock market and actively finding a new incremental market. The old saying: "Divide the cake is better to make the cake bigger together." Increasing the consumption capacity of low -income people and the cooperation and construction of countries along the "Belt and Road" countries will become a new engine of the incremental market. Of course All foreign investment needs to participate together.

There are still many uncertainty in the future of China and Germany. Slowing speed, adjusting strategies, and finding new directions, maybe they can run further.

FT社评：德国的经济模式需要更新 (Free Version)

Authors: ['']

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》

Time: 2023-06-19T06:59:46+00:00

Published Time: 2023-06-18T12:00:99+08:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T02:58:99+08:00

Description: The current geopolitical adversity highlights the vulnerability of the international economic model pursued by Germany, and it also highlights its challenges in the medium and long term.

Images: ["000182828_pic..."]

Themes: ['德国经济', '关注']

Keywords: ['德国经济', '制造业', '工业', '能源', '供应链']

Type: Article

Warm reminder from FT Chinese website: If you are interested in the content of more FT Chinese website, please search for "FT Chinese Network" in Apple App Store or Google Application Market and download the official applications of FT Chinese website.

Data recently released by Germany show that the prospect of this European economic power is dim. The German economy has declined this year, and the country's emotions have recently decreased as the fastest speed since the epidemic. OECD(OECD)It is now expected that Germany's economic growth rate will be the lowest in major economies this year. However, the trend after this year is even more worrying. The current geopolitical adversity -the upgrade of tensions from Russia's invasion of Ukraine to the United States and China -highlight the vulnerability of the international economic model pursued by Germany, and also highlights its challenges in the medium and long term.

German Chancellor Olaf Tumz(Olaf Scholz)It has always been ambitious to re -adjust its economic direction, including reducing Germany's dependence on Russia's energy and creating a new industrial supply chain. The Souls government has been acting quickly. Increased the target of renewable energy power generation to 80%, increasing the attractiveness of Germany as a green investment destination. Germany will invest tens of billions of dollars to promote the development of the semiconductor industry. The German economy also showed toughness, and it did not come true for the terrible predictions of its deep recession this year. But the future tasks are still arduous.

Germany has rapidly reduced its dependence on Russia's natural gas. The rapid construction of liquefied natural gas terminals help enhance energy security. However, the decision to close the last nuclear reactor in Germany in April, and the slow promotion of renewable energy, means that Germany still rely on imports and fossil fuels to meet its energy needs, and it is still subject to international prices that are easy to fluctuate.

Economic diversification is also challenging. Manufacturing accounts for about a quarter of German output. The automobile manufacturing industry as a key industry has been declining since 2018. Germany's expertise in internal combustion engine technology has been challenged by automotive electrification transformation, and China has an advantage in the field. It is not simple to "de -risk" in China (China is the largest commodity and trade partner country in Germany), because many German companies believe that China is a vital market and a key supplier of intermediate products.

Shuortz called for the transformation with a new "German speed". But he needed to remove many "deceleration bands" that hindered the German economy for a long time. Renewable energy infrastructure projects such as wind power field have been dragged down by the lengthy planning process. The reform has been launched. Business leaders complained that heavy bureaucracy, high energy costs and limited digitalization have also hindered vitality. Since the establishment of SAP companies more than 50 years ago, there has not been a world -class German technology company.

The shortage of labor is another obstacle. It is expected that in Germany to have a gap of up to 7 million by 2035, part of the reason is that the population aging is aging. The construction industry, electrical engineering, and professional services are lacking in skilled labor, and these industries are important for the country's economic ambitions. The revision of immigration regulations is ongoing. Reforming the economy also requires more public investment and incentives, but the demand for funds will be limited to the promise of population aging and improving national defense expenditure. The disputes within the government also dragged their hind legs.

In a sense, Germany is the victim of its own achievements. In the era of rapid globalization in the 20 years after the collapse of the Berlin Wall, its economic model is prosperous. But the times are changing, and the foundation of its past competitiveness and toughness has been challenged. The economic and disadvantages of the supply of regulatory, digitalization, and labor supply seem to be so urgent when they are in good time, but now they are restricting the flexibility of the country's economy. Only by solving these deep obstacles facing economic growth can Germany complete self -renewal again.

Translator/He Li

News Source: http://www.ftchinese.com/story/001100012

Poet Yang Lian: Migrant worker poets are real exiles in China ｜ Views

Author: None

Publisher: Radio Free Asia (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-19T07:00:00-04:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-16T18:50:58-04:00

Description: None

Radio of Liberty Asia

Moderator: Hello everyone, this is "view" I am Tang Qiwei. Today, the "Viewpoint" program connected through the video and visited Mr. Yang Lian, a famous poet in Berlin. In the 1980s, Yang Lian made a sensation in the poetry of mainland China with the long poem "Noigon". In 1987, he was selected as one of the "Top Ten Poets" by his readers. In 2018, Yang Lian won the Hungarian International Poetry Award, known as the "Poetry Award", and became the first Chinese poet to win this award. Yang Lian has a quarter of Mongolian descent. His grandmother is the first generation of Mongolian people who can marry the Han nationality. His father was the Shantong family of Beijing Auspicious Theater. Peking opera master Mei Lanfang sang red in the auspicious theater. After 1949, Yang Lian's parents were sent to work at the Swiss Chinese Embassy and were born in Switzerland. Yang Lian was born, and did not return to Beijing to live in Beijing until the age of six.

Reporter: I found that your life is very special. What does the family have the greatest influence on you during your growth?

Yang Lian: Of course, my father is a very loving culture, especially literature. In -penetrating in his literary hobbies, there is a kind of pursuit of conscience and this character. My mother is the background of Shanghai, and her family is a family like the old Shanghai film industry. My mother's pro -mys are the famous film director named Shi Dongshan (directed "Eight Thousand Miles Road Clouds and Moon", "New Children's Heroes", etc.). Suicide and die one of Chinese intellectuals. The day of his death was the second day when I was born on February 23, 1955, so I had to think that at this point, the background of my mother's house was also deeply related to me.

Reporter: I remember that you said that the death of your mother at the age of 20 is a starting point for your creation. Why?

Yang Lian: Of course, under the influence of my parents, I have liked literature and art from childhood. It's just some publicity. On January 7, 1976, my mother died suddenly myocardial infarction, because at that time they lacked medical medicine in their dry school. My mother also gave me a starting point for the year of my life at the lowest point in my life. In that year, I had a conversation with me to talk to me with me. And these texts present a completely different amount of things than those previously painted things. So in fact, my mother's death also gave me the second birth, the birth of poetry.

Reporter: I know that your creation is very affected by your mother's death. What literary style has your initial creation be influenced?

Yang Lian: In a sense of my creation, I came from detour. Unlike these poets of other hazy poetry, they were a small circle in Beijing at that time, including North Island, including Gu Cheng. They all came into contact with some modern literary works in the West, such as ( Spanish poet) Lorga and so on. But I went to the village directly from the university, so I didn't have the opportunity to contact these things. But just as I just said, in 1976, after having the painful life experience that could be said to be, it was increasingly feeling that such a false and empty newspaper had nothing to do with my real life. Then we cut into the village in that village. The life of the real people is also a very important classroom for me. The kind of love and hate, such a kind of entangled and complicated feelings between people and land. In fact, I discovered that it was not my feelings alone, but a very profound feelings in China that can be said to be said to be a very profound emotion in the entire historical and cultural tradition, and even poetic traditions. But this all requires me in the middle of the reading and thinking in the middle, and go against these experiences again. *

Reporter: In 1983, you announced that Chang Shi Nonorng caused a sensation in Chinese poetry. At that time, you were only in your twenties. How would you evaluate your famous work now?

Yang Lian: In fact, this poem is famous, let's say that. Whether it is because of criticism, or it does have the amount of poetry, but I really think it is a turning point in my life. Such a mad state of completely anti -common sense cannot be just a result of a man. In fact, at that time, a poetry magazine, others said that the representative of the hazy poetry was Gu Cheng, and that person said something to calculate with Guo Cheng. Because they suddenly found that such poetry had been far from such a small flower and grass style, just in the sense of the wind and snow, I spent the singing or moaning. At the same time, in 1983, this so -called political movement that was criticized by my poem was criticized by this poem. In fact, this has a greater significance, because people suddenly found that at that time, it was a Mao Zedong's thoughts without Mao Zedong. From that time, I have completely transformed such a spiritual energy of literature from a surface socially social to a kind of inner, a kind of question or inquiry about self, and turned it into the energy of creation.

Moderator: Compared with Chinese poets, Yang Lian has long highlighted different creative personality with the practice of its grand historical subjects. However, because of the five poets of Yang Lian, Beimao, Gu Cheng, Shu Ting, and Jianghe published in 1986, Yang Lian is generally considered to be one of the representatives of the Chinese hazy poetry school.

Reporter: Just now you mentioned hazy poems, I know that you and Gucheng Shuting, Beimao, and Guicheng, and Jianghe in the 1980s. Why is it called hazy poetry? How will you evaluate the impact of the era of hazy poetry?Reporter: I saw (about) the biography of the poet Haizi mentioned that he was particularly affected by you at the beginning of his creation. How would you evaluate his poems and the last tragedy of Haizi?

Yang Lian: I think he thinks he is of course a very talented young poet. For me, he has also come to my house to talk to us. He is a very ambitious poet. If he is fake, let him go through the process of life and thinking, I believe he will develop much more. But Haizi, the sensitive of his poet, can be said to die in March 1989, and it was only one month away from the students on the street in April 1989. (He) It can be said to be like a radar of a Chinese society. One of people who are ahead of the vast majority, a sound, heard a sound as an restlessness in the air in the air, and feels that rhythm. As a sensitive mind, it may be exactly exactly stimulating him, because the person who heard such a sound earlier, the surrounding environment is relatively more depressed to him, because he has not moved around. The earliest rabbit or the cat who felt the earthquake was coming. But one situation that was not moved around was crushed. In fact, he is really a pioneer of the whole movement. In my opinion, he is particularly significant in this aspect of Chinese society and ideology.

Reporter: Speaking of 1984, I saw that after June 4th, I wrote a poem called 1989. The ending sentence at the end is: This is nothing more than a common year. Why do you have such a sigh?

Yang Lian: Because it was not an emergency for me for me. From the end of 1976 (Cultural Revolution), we began to wake up, to the underground publication of the Democratic Wall in 1978, and to clear mental pollution in 1983 and all a series of political movements around it, such as opposing bourgeois liberalization. The control and suppression of ideas throughout the 1980s, and the awakening of the younger generation has always been relative movement and always collided. And the progressive deepening of each level, I just said that the political reality, historical and cultural language self, and the entry of such a level one by one is actually constantly injecting new ideological energy and accumulating new social shocks into this society. And the progress of such a level of energy, in 1988, we already felt that the air was covered with gunpowder. When the Australian Art Committee invited me to visit for a year in 1988, it was actually the year when we set up a survivor poet club. In fact, (we) had clearly felt such a close storm, come to me to me Saying this is an inevitable result of a series of processes. If I am in Beijing, I will definitely be on the square, but when the whole world is crying for it, at this time, I actually have a question in my heart. I said that if we think Tiananmen as a massacre and a large -scale death we see for the first time, then where are we remembering the disaster of all the dead before? If we tears, just brushing our memories of death again and again, then who can guarantee that today's tears are not preparing for the new shock of the future? So this is nothing more than ordinary year. In fact, I transferred this question from an external inquiry to me to my own inside. If we actually, in 1989 it was just an ordinary year in our lives, then how we will face it, such a normal and catastrophic life. In fact, in this ordinary year today, it has become very ordinary.

Reporter: Just now you mentioned the survivor, I saw that you said that all our works after Tiananmen slaughtered, whether they were written at home or abroad, can only be called survivor literature. why?

Yang Lian: Because when we were preparing to set up one in 1988, when we were still young poets such as young poets, this survivor more referred to a spiritual survivor, whether we can survive in spirit. However, no one expected that less than a year after we established the survivor poet club, the reality caught up with this word. After Tiananmen (incident), each of us can't get around, we must remember that every new sentence we write, starting from here. So the survivor has become at this time, and all of our writing starting points.

Moderator: In the mid -to -late 1980s, after experiencing the fate of poetry criticism and banning poetry, a large number of poets in mainland China across the world and wandered around the world. Many of them have returned to China for so many years, and Yang Lian finally settled in London and Berlin.

Reporter: Let's talk about Gu Cheng, because you also mentioned Gu Cheng just now. I know you met in your early twenties, and then you have a lot of contacts after immigration to New Zealand. Gu Cheng is known as a fairy tale poet, but in the end his ending was so violent and cruel. What do you think of Gu Cheng's tragedy?

Yang Lian: When Gu Cheng became famous, he used publicity as a banner. If you only read his text, of course, it is very pure and bright fairy tales created by sterling silver, but in fact, I think there is a kind of violence that he has always contained in Chinese society in the other side. It is an authoritarian tendency. So in fact, I think this personality tragedy highlights the intricate splitting of each individual (existing) in China.

Reporter: As a poet, how would you evaluate Gu Cheng's poems? Because you also mentioned just now that his poems are relatively pure and more pure, what about the depth and thickness you are pursuing?

Yang Lian: This is very interesting. Of course, I still like his poems very much, from the perspective of his aura. Especially if he is 13 years old, you can write: Closing your eyes, the world has nothing to do with me. But our lives are not always kept. In such a fairy tale, especially when we are forced to leave China and become an exile person, at this time, the inner endurance of a poet will increase infinitely. It can be said that myself (1993) the place where the sea stopped, that is, the year when Gu Cheng died. In that year, I stopped through the sea. For the first time I used a relatively large structure overseas to integrate my wandering experience, and finally implemented a sentence, to overlook myself from the shore. All external wandering is actually part of our inner wandering. At this time, I suddenly felt, okay, I found my own thinking and basic ways and basic ways of life today. But looking back, if I look at a batch of poems written between 1992 and 93, whether at that time or ghosts or ghosts, his language has a very violent state. This inner crushing state is almost consistent with Gu Cheng's later heart. This language is a fragmented fragment.

Reporter: So in 1993, you created the place where the sea stopped. At that time, you also said that this was the darkest moment in your exile. But just now I hear you say that this poem is actually the stop of the sea, let you go out of this darkest? Moderator: Since going abroad in 1988, Yang Lian has never stopped creating. According to geographical changes, he divided his manuscripts into three parts: "Chinese Manuscripts", "South Pacific Manuscripts" and "European Manuscripts". After completing the masterpiece of the "South Pacific Manuscript" period, "Where the Sea Stop", at the end of 1996, Yang Lian began his "European Manuscript" creation.

Yang Lian: At that time, there was no place to live, and wandering has become a real life state of life, but in such a state of walking around, in fact The difference between different languages in different countries is increasingly diluted, and it is increasingly discovered that in fact, different places and different languages and even the depths of different languages and culture. The big difference, even this is not only the same generation, that is, in the deeper level of ancient and modern China and foreign countries, we all have a convergence point. After the feeling of stopping me in the sea, I started writing another poem called concentric circle. You can think of the word concentric circle. In fact, life literature is a kind of concentric circle. The heart is constantly questioning the poetry. The living environment has become our concentric in life.

Moderator: Before 2014 to the epidemic, Yang Lian was invited to become a specially appointed professor at the School of Literature of Shantou University in Guangdong Province, and had the opportunity to communicate face to face with young Chinese students. In 2017, "Survivor" was repeated in mainland China. As one of the editor -in -chief, Yang Lian also went to Beijing to participate in the repetition ceremony. From 1988 Survivor Club's Poetry of Oil Seal, to thirty years later, it was repeatedly published in the form of the Internet. In Yang Lian's view, this is also a kind of "concentric circle".

Reporter: I know that you have also taught a book in European universities. How will you compare the attitude of Chinese young people and young European people to poetry? What does poetry mean for them today?

Yang Lian: I think there are about 40 students in my class each year, at least five or six, which makes me feel that the future can be a good seed of poetry. Many of these students are from the background of rural families. The works I write make me feel that they directly have a deep relationship with the source of life like the family and their own life. In a sense, they may also add such an influence with classical poetry. So they have such a poem that can be said to be the foundation. In this regard, when I think I recite poetry abroad, or when they are exposed to young people abroad, I think they may be less. I said that I like me to study, and it is good to read.

Reporter: I think it is particularly interesting to have a phenomenon you just mentioned. You said that you have several students in the class when teaching. You feel very aura. Most of them are from rural areas. In your opinion, why are these children from rural areas, and there are many poems of migrant workers' poems, but they will be even more moving?

Yang Lian: Because poetry should move the easiest point of the people, or the most fundamental point is sincerity. If poetry loses sincerity, then it has become a very meaningless thing. Regardless of the children from these rural areas, the parents who see their parents can make money through quite hard labor, to make money for them to go to school, let alone the poets of these migrant workers. The exiles in China have left their hometown of hot soil, and in a place for them to make money much more than we go abroad for them to go abroad. In fact, these people have accumulated the deep sourness of life in their hearts, especially the poetry of these migrant workers. When our survivor (poem) issued invitations to all Chinese poetry, I was actually very surprised to find that among these poets, there are some strange names that are completely strange, but these works are better than all than all than all. Those names I know, or some of the works I have used to get more and more moving, because they have the first -hand experience of living or even bloody, and then they have not been in the low -level publicity at all. The slogan is looking for your own expression. For example, Xu Lizhi, who has already died, for example, you are still alive Guo Jinniu . These poems are really touched by the Chinese foreigners.

Reporter: Yes, I read the terracotta warriors and horses of Xu Lizhi (on the current), and I felt very shocking.

Yang Lian: He is a pity that he did not contribute to the survivors, and he became the fourteenth (committed to committing suicide) in Fuji. And what I was even more moved was that thousands of these parts wearing blue workers facing the crowd and standing next to the machine were all part of these parts of the machine. We originally thought they were silent. When they turned their faces, they turned their faces. When we came, we suddenly found that they had sounds and very personalized voices, and there was a kind of vivid sound in the middle of Chinese literature, that is, I saw China in these people. I saw China in China The tradition of poetry for more than 3,000 years has not been cut off, and it continues to move forward.

Moderator: Mr. Yang Lian said that today's poetry is an era of individual poetics. Poetry sinks the bottom of the sea, and it is dark and calmly looking at the dangerous world of storms. For more of Mr. Yang Lian's point of view, please pay attention to the next program. I am Tang Qiwei, thank you for watching, and you will see it again.

Employees should not be dressed, should be low -key

In October last year, Chinese President Xi Jinping mentioned in the 20th report that "resolutely win anti -corruption struggleTackling the battle for a long time. "

According to the website of the Central Discipline Inspection Commission of the Communist Party of China (Central Discipline Inspection Commission), Li Xi, the secretary of the Central Discipline Inspection Commission in January this year, listed the financial industry, state -owned enterprises, political and legal industries such as "centralized power, dense funds, and resources" as the The focus of rectification of corruption, and said that it is necessary to correct the "hedonism, extravagant wind"; in February, the Central Discipline Inspection Commission also published an article, Emphasize Break the "Financial Elite theory", "only money theory", "Western reading theory"Essence

Reuters pointed out that Beijing's attitude prompts financial companies to take action. Whether state -owned enterprises or private owners, they are ensuring that they have not violated the government's ideology.

An employee of a large state -owned common fund in China revealed to Reuters that the company asked them not to upload photos of high -end diet, clothes or bags on social media, try not to attract the attention of regulatory units and avoid public criticism. Another medium -sized bank employee said that when the company wants them to wear luxury brands or memorize brand bags when they go to work, they cannot live in a five -star hotel when they are on a business trip. Another person familiar with the matter also said that the senior management of a state -owned insurance company was told that he could not wear expensive clothes to work.

Financial practitioners are one of the highest income groups in China. However, due to the recent influence of Beijing's anti -corruption movement, many operators require employees to avoid wearing high -end clothing. (Experience diagram)

Salary and bonus

According to two sources who are unwilling to name, the Industrial and Commercial Bank of China and the Construction Bank of China intend to reduce the allowance of the bank's headquarters employees from this year. They said that the summer allowance of about 1,500 yuan to 2,000 yuan per month was canceled from this month. None of these two banks responded to Reuters' comment requests.

In early June, Reuters reported that CITIC Securities is cutting the salary of the investment banking department, reducing the basic salary by 15%; the company's competitors and China International Financial Co., Ltd. also cut the investment banking department's bonus this year by 30% To 50%.

"Caixin Weekly" also pointed out in April that from the annual report of listed companies in China in 2022, it can be seen that "the average salary of many listed securities firms fell by 20 % compared with the previous year, and the executives decreased by more than 30 % ... Although the overall salary of the banking industry has changed Not big, but the salary of executives has declined significantly; the trust industry not only declines in the overall salary level, but also has a significant layoff. "

The financial regulatory agency is an example?

Under the driving force of Xi Jinping's promotion of "common prosperity" and anti -corruption, China has recently launched the reform of financial regulatory agencies.

According to the institutional reform plan in 2023The CCP has once again formed the "Central Financial Working Committee" to strengthen the party's guidance of the financial system. The State Council of China established the "State Financial Supervision and Administration Administration" in May, based on the original "Bank of China Insurance Supervision and Administration Commission" (China Banking Regulatory Commission).

China implemented a large -scale institutional reform earlier this year, and financial regulatory units have since formed a "one line, one game and one time" pattern, namely the People's Bank of China (central bank), the State Financial Supervision and Administration Administration, and the China Securities Regulatory Commission (Securities Regulatory Commission).

According to Reuters last month, after the institutional reform, the CSRC and the People's Bank of China have reduced their salary budgets in 2023. Bloomberg analyzed the budget report of the Securities Regulatory Commission that the unit's salary and allowance budget for employees this year was 17%less than the previous year. Those who are familiar with the matter have revealed that some employees may be reduced by more than 50%. Earlier, those who worked at financial supervision units had higher salaries than ordinary Chinese civil servants.Xinsun, a senior lecturer in China and East Asia Business, the King's College London, told Reuters: "The economic growth momentum and the overall budget of the government are not as good as in the past. That is a key political priority, and it is also the most important driving force for the recent tightening policy. "

"China's inequality has reached a high level, which has been continued for a long time." Sun Xin said that the Chinese Communist Party is now reducing the benefits of the "financial elite" to reduce the inequality in the regime. To achieve political stability.

The United Nations will protect the marine ecology through the historic Gonghai Treaty

Publisher: 法新社

Published Time: 2023-06-19T09:32:09+00:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T09:20:06+00:00

Description: (Agence France -Presse, New York, New York, 19th) The United Nations will today through the world's first international treaty to protect the sea. The purpose of this historic environmental agreement is to protect the marine ecosystem that is vital to humans.

Videos: []

Images: ["000000.png"]

Lizkaran, a member of the non -governmental organization "Pew Charitable Trusts" (Pew Charitable Trusts), told AFP that "this will be a major achievement. We have celebrated the text of the text in March. But (the treaty (treaty ) After passing, I really pave the way for a step. "

This milematic, The High Seas Treaty will establish a legal structure to expand the scope of environmental protection to an international waters that account for more than 60 % of the world's ocean area.

After more than 15 years of discussion, including 4 years of official negotiations. The UN member states have been finalized in the final marathon negotiation in March this year, and the text of the treaty is finalized.

A group of scientists wrote in the medical magazine "Lancet": "The healthy ocean, from coastal waters to remote public sea, to the deep sea bed area, are an indispensable part of human health, well -being, and survival."

Because there are a large number of oceans in the world in the jurisdiction of the exclusive economic zone of individual countries, the protection tasks of "Gonghai" require international cooperation.

The "Gonghai Treaty" of the "Gonghai Treaty" refers to the international waters that all countries have the right to fish, navigate and do research. At present, only 1%of Gonghai is protected.

Governments of various countries passed a historic agreement in Montreal in Montreal, Canada last December to agree to protect 30%of the world's land and oceans worldwide by 2030. For this goal, the Gonghai Treaty is very important.

The non -governmental organization believes that after the UN General Assembly passed the treaty, the approval of 60 member states to take effect can be achieved. This threshold should be achieved, because there were about 50 "High AmbitionCoality" that promoted the Gonghai Treaty. Countries, including EU countries, Chile, Mexico, India and Japan.

However, there are 193 member states in the United Nations, 60 countries are generally adopted by countries, and there is still a way to go.

The High Seas Alliance (High Seas Alliance) issued a post on a community platform Twitter (Twitter) appealed: "(Gonghai Treaty) quickly approves and takes into effect." It is important!"

Safety issues may be the top priority of discussion. American officials are increasingly worried that friction with the Chinese army around the sea of China. The United States is also paying close attention to the establishment of military bases in Asia, Africa and the Middle East, and warns China not to provide lethal military assistance to Russia.

Kangda(Daniel J.Kritenbrink)Said that Brintken intends to discuss with Chinese officials that the two countries may have common interests, including climate change and global economic stability.

Blingken may also ask China to release several American citizens who have been detained, imprisoned or prohibited from exporting, and tried to restart some civil exchanges, which may include increasing the number of journalist visas issued by the two countries to each other. Before the deterioration of US -China relations, I agreed to increase the current number of journalist visas.

After the Sunday talks, Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs spokesman Hua Chunying said on Twitter that the two countries "welcome more students, scholars and business people to visit each other."

U.S. officials also said that they are expected to discuss with China to restrict the export of material for the manufacture of Fennea, and Fentney has caused fatal addiction in the United States and other countries. The two countries may also agree to allow more direct flights between them. After meeting with Qin Gang on Sunday, officials of the State Council said that the two sides had agreed to establish a working group on these issues and other issues.

Blintken and Qin Gang held talks at the Diaoyutai State Guest in Beijing Sunday. POOL Photo by Leah Millis

What can China be mentioned?

China is expected to put forward a series of dissatisfaction that reflects Beijing's views. The Chinese government believes that the United States is the hegemon that is declining, and is determined to curb China in terms of economic, military and diplomacy to maintain its status.

advertise

The head of the list of China is the Taiwan issue. Beijing claims that this independent island is its own territory, and the United States has given Taiwan military assistance.

Chinese leader Xi Jinping described Taiwan as "the core of China's core interests" and accused the United States of supporting the "Taiwan independence" forces and interfered with China's internal affairs.

China may also be highly dissatisfied with the efforts of the United States and restricting China to obtain advanced semiconductor chips and manufacturing equipment. The United States said that in order to prevent US technology from falling into the Chinese army, it is necessary to take restrictions. This restriction may delay China's technological development for many years. China regards restrictions on the ban as an example of "zero and competition", and believes that this competition is promoting the confrontation between the two countries.China's ultimate goal is to treat China as the same country as the same country, so that it has an equal right to speak on the global stage, so as not to feel that the US military existence in Asia pose a threat to itself.

Will Xi Jinping meet Brinken?

advertise

Xi Jinping may meet with Brinken. When the Trump administration's second Secretary of State Mike Ponzhi's European visit in 2018, he met with him. However, officials on both sides have been formulated the final details of the Blingken schedule in the past week. Whether the two may meet at the last moment may be determined, and a large extent depends on the talks on Sunday and Monday morning.

However, the two had previously talked. Blinden had seen Xi Jinping on many occasions, including accompanied by Biden to visit Beijing and Chengdu in 2011. Biden served as Vice President of the United States at the time. Security consultant.

The US State Department stated in a press release on Sunday that Bollingin invited Qin Gang to Washington, and the two agreed to arrange for visit.

South Korea's 60 -year -old employment population is higher than in his 20s, the employment population

Images: []

Type: NewsArticle

Breadcrumbs: ['即时', '国际']

According to data released by the National Statistics Portal of the South Korean Department of Statistics on Monday (June 19), the employment population between 60 and 69 in South Korea was 3.833 million in the employment population of 20 to 29 years old in May.

The Yonhap News Agency reported that in May, the employment population in the 60s in South Korea has exceeded the age of 20 for three consecutive years since 2021.

The employment population in his 60s was 3.598 million, less than 3.602 million employment population in his 20s, but since 2021, the number of employment in his 20s began. In other words, more than 60 people who are working are more than 20 years old, which reflects changes in population structures such as aging.

Also based on May, the 60 -year -old population in South Korea was 5.709 million in 2018, less than 6.382 million people in their 20s, but in 2021, the population increased to 6.887 million in 2021, and began to be more than 20 years old. (6.481 million).

Since five years since 2018, South Korea's 60 -year -old population has increased by 1.772 million, while the population in his 20s has decreased by 227,000. Recently, as the "baby tide" generation enters the age of aging, the population over 60 years of age has increased rapidly.

In addition, the increase in the increase of the elderly who make money to make up for the family is also the reason for the increase in the employment population in their 60s.

According to a survey by the South Korean Department of Statistics, the proportion of people from 60 to 69 years old hopes to continue working, from 66.3%in May 2018 to 71.8%in May 2022. The reason for the "replenishment" is the highest in 2018 and 2022.

The employment rate of 20 to 29 in the same period was 62.3%, an increase of 0.9 percentage points year -on -year. Although the employment population decreased by 63,000 year -on -year, the employment rate rose, which reflects the changes in the Korean population structure. The South Korean government believes that the young labor market situation is better.

The European Union has developed a risk -going strategy

(Voice of Germany) on Tuesday, the European Commission will announce a "economic security" strategy. Reuters reported that a series of measures of the European Commission include reviewing foreign investment and export controls, which aims to prevent China and other countries from getting valuable technologies from the European Union and prevent related technologies from being used by competitors for military use. The European Commission will introduce the "economic security" strategy to EU members and member states. Next week, the European Union will also hold a meeting in Brussels to discuss relations with China.

According to the German "Business Daily", the basic elements of this strategy include more stringent investment supervision and export restrictions, research and development of auditing mechanisms involved in security, and creating more tough supply chains. Bloomberg specifically pointed out that there are currently 5 types of tools in the European Union that can be used to suppress China's geopolitical rise, which are anti -economic coercion measures, supervise and control the EU's overseas investment, strictly review foreign investment in the EU, Hong Kong strategy, and promote the trade agreement. Essence

Anti -economic stress

The Voice of Germany earlier this month has reported that the representatives of the EU Parliament and the government representatives of various member states will be a new anti -economic coercion toolReach consensus. In the future, if the third country tries to interfere with the political decision of the EU or its member states with improper economic sanctions, the EU will be able to counter the country's improving punitive tariffs. Other response methods also include restricting the country's direct investment in the European Union and bidding in public projects in the European Union. In addition, the European Union also stated that restrictions on the relevant transactions of the service industry will also become possible sanctions.

Over the past few years, the EU and its member states have become the target of economic coercion of the EU foreign countries many times. For example, China has implemented trade restrictions on Lithuania. The European Union believes that such restrictions do not comply with the relevant provisions of the World Trade Organization, and also have a joint impact on the EU's internal market exports.

In the face of Chinese investment, how should Europe be dealt with?

Vice Chairman of the European Commission, Valdisdombrovskis, vice chairman of the EU Commission, said that sanctions should only be used as the last means when they are unsuccessful. Non -EU countries have dialogue. When the dialogue is unsuccessful, the possibility of mediation, arbitration or judicial trial should also be considered.

investment and export

Next month, a new regulations on foreign subsidies will begin to take effect, which will give the European Commission's power to prevent foreign -containing opponents who have obtained subsidies in other countries in unfair benefits in the EU market. Bloomberg reports that the tool stipulates the reporting obligation to all companies involved in large EU public bidding or mergers and acquisitions transactions.

Key infrastructure

The European Parliament will also consider making new restrictions on foreign companies that intend to invest in key European infrastructure. Chinese companies have owned shares in the ports of at least 10 EU member states. Since last year, Hamburg PortThe plan of a container terminal caused huge controversy in Germany, which also led to a wave of approval procedures. The final project was approved, but China had to reduce the proportion of equity. A factor of "error decision" focused by critics is that the whaper is not listed as "key infrastructure" in Hamburg Port.

Trading Agreement and Global Portal

In order to reduce its dependence on China's supply chain, the European Union is negotiating and signing a trade agreement with Chile and Australia, which will help the EU's key material for electric vehicle batteries-lithium. The European Commission is also negotiating an agreement with the Southern Common Market Trade Group, including Argentina, Brazil, Uruguay, and Paraguay.

In addition, the European Union launched its "Global Portal" initiative to respond to China's "Belt and Road" plan to improve its economic influence in Latin America, Central Asia and Africa. The initiative plans to invest 300 billion euros, mainly for infrastructure investment.

High interest rates are not "free version"

Authors: ['为英国《金融时报》撰稿']

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》

Time: 2023-06-19T12:15:02+00:00

Published Time: 2023-06-18T12:00:99+08:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T08:12:99+08:00

Description: Malcov: How long can the Fed and other central banks still put anti -anti -inflation on maintaining financial stability? The transition of policy makers priority may be earlier than many investors imagined.

Images: ["000180163_pic..."]

Themes: ['金融市场', '关注']

Keywords: ['货币政策', '利率', '中央银行', '美联储', '债券', '金融市场']

Type: Article

Warm reminder from FT Chinese website: If you are interested in the content of more FT Chinese website, please search for "FT Chinese Network" in Apple App Store or Google Application Market and download the official applications of FT Chinese website.

The author of this article is Patek asset management(Pictet Asset Management)Senior economist

Poor bond investor. After suffering the devastating losses of dual digits in 2022, the fixed income market is still more fragile than any time since the subprime crisis. Estimated by the volatility of the bond price of the bonds closely tracked(MOVE)The index has recently touched the highest level in the past 15 years.

What is even more worrying is that the instability of US Treasury bonds, as a gang rails in the global bond market, is particularly obvious.

In just one week in March this year, the two -year US Treasury yield raised the largest single -day decline since the collapse of the stock market in 1987, and the largest single -day increase since 2009. This is not a manifestation of defensive asset categories.

Indeed, in view of the radical measures taken by central banks in various countries to overcome inflation, the bond market is destined to suffer turbulence. In the United States, the fastest speed since the 1980s has risen since the 1980s, and in just 14 months, it has increased from zero to 5%to 5.25%in just 14 months.

However, the recent violent fluctuations in the market show that there is a new motivation. We believe that bond holders have become the core conflict of the central bank's policy formulation.

The current problem is the Federal Reserve(Fed)And other central banks can also put anti -anti -inflation in another official mission -how long to maintain financial stability -how long.

In our opinion, the transformation of the preferred matters of policy makers may be earlier than many investors think earlier. The interest rate has risen to the point where the debt crisis may cause the debt crisis; maybe it won't be long, the interest rate will be lowered, which will cause a rebound in the bond market.

This is the conclusion that we have obtained by analyzing the trend of public and private debt in major economies in the world. Although the economic recovery after the epidemic has helped reduce government debt and GDP in China last year(GDP)The ratio of debt to economic output is still much higher than the level of 2020.

It wandered around 96%of GDP. However, what is even more concerned is that in many developed countries, the number of public and private debt is growing in a long -term unsustainable speed.

In order to evaluate the vulnerability of a country's debt crisis, we compare the current growth rate of a country's public and private debt to GDP with the long -term historical trend. The higher the average level, the more vulnerable to a country is affected by debt liquidation.

Analysis shows that economies such as the United States and the euro zone are in a potential dangerous situation. At the end of 2022, the ratio of credit to GDP of these two economies was 268.2%and 254.2%, respectively.

According to our calculations, if the United States wants to make its debt burden sustainable for a long time, the cost of borrowing needs to be reduced by about 1.5 percentage points. For the euro area, the required decline is even greater because it is because of the unstable public finance in Italy. We found that the interest rate level of the entire euro area is nearly 3 percentage points higher than the level required to avoid the credit crisis.

Perhaps it is surprising that Switzerland is also close to the dangerous threshold, and the ratio of credit to GDP reaches 315.1%. Our model shows that in Switzerland, as long as we have a moderate interest rate hike twice, it will threaten the country's long -term debt status.

All this does not mean that the central bank will suddenly change the string and start to reduce the cost of borrowing.

However, as the global debt level is much higher than the outbreak of the new crown epidemic, policy makers will understand the risk of further interest rate hikes.

European Central Bank(ECB)In the recent semi -annual "Financial Stability Evaluation"(Financial Stability Review)It also admits this.

The European Central Bank warned in the report that the recent monetary policy tightened the "cracks and vulnerability" of the entire financial system. It said that rising interest rates have begun to put pressure on governments, enterprises and families in the entire European region, and the real estate market seems to be particularly affected.

Therefore, for bond investors, the conclusion is that this period of high interest rates may eventually be not a new normal they are preparing to welcome, but may soon be proven to be an exception.

Weilai joined the bloody price war, and the electric vehicle industry's section (Free Version)

Authors: ['']

Publisher: 英国《金融时报》

Time: 2023-06-19T12:22:18+00:00

Published Time: 2023-06-18T12:00:99+08:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T08:22:99+08:00

Description: Although small -scale new energy vehicle companies such as Weilai are reduced, they are almost helpless to prevent their market share from flowing to greater competitors such as BYD and Tesla.

Images: ["000184157_pic..."]

Themes: ['专栏', '咏竹坊', '关注']

Keywords: ['咏竹坊', '蔚来', '蔚来汽车', '电动汽车', '威马', '小鹏汽车']

Type: Article

Warm reminder from FT Chinese website: If you are interested in the content of more FT Chinese website, please search for "FT Chinese Network" in Apple App Store or Google Application Market and download the official applications of FT Chinese website.

Weilai Group(NIO.US;9866.HK)It has always been widely praised for its advanced electric vehicle, but last week it found that it was facing an unprecedented situation because it announced that it was an object of a netizen laughed at after the announcement of the price of all electric vehicles by 30,000 yuan. Just two months ago, Li Bin, CEO of Weilai, also claimed that he would definitely not join the price war that is currently stifling the industry, saying that this blind price reduction will only lead to "malignant competition."

Weilai's transformation highlights the current dilemma of Chinese electric car companies, because they are trying to go through an unexpected change, and analysis agencies say that this change may continue for a while. The situation of small companies is the most difficult, because further price cuts will erode their meager profits. But refusing to participate in this price reduction game, it will face the sales flow to BYD(1211.hk; 002594)Tesla(TSLA.US)Waiting for industry giants to risk.

Let's look at the recent price war, how can we affect the ideal car including the ideal car(LI.US; 2015.HK), Zero Running Cars(9863.HK)He Xiaopeng Automobile(XPEV.US;9868.HK)And Weimar Automobile, Chinese local small electric car companies. But first of all, we have to look back at how this price war has continued for months, how it evolved.

Everything started in October last year. At that time, Tesla raised the price of its Model 3 and Model at a maximum of 9%. By January of this year, the price reduced further, a maximum of 13.5%. The two rounds of price reductions have prompted other companies to follow suit. Among them, Xiaopeng Automobile announced in January that the G3I SUV and P5 and P7 cars had a maximum price reduction of 13%. BYD joined the following month. In 2021, the "Han EV" model was reduced by 20,000 yuan in Beijing. The 2021 style "Qin EV" model was reduced by 15,000 yuan.

Other brands, from domestic giants such as GAC, SAIC, FAW, to foreign brands such as Ford, Volkswagen, BMW, and Toyota, they also joined this bloody battle. Before the price cut, the Chinese government canceled a major electric vehicle purchase incentive plan at the end of last year. Earlier, the plan had helped the industry sales in 2022.

This price war also spread to the field of fuel vehicles, and major car companies were anxious to clean up the inventory before the new emission standard took effect in July.

According to data from the domestic media First Financial, the third -party consulting company Lisi strategic positioning consultation data said that as of the end of March, more than 40 car brands had been involved in this price war, and launched electric vehicles and fuel vehicles subsidies or price reductions. The data compiled by another domestic news media product "China Automobile Market" stated that with the increase in price cuts, about 20%of the passenger cars sold in China reached or exceeded 10,000 yuan.

Promote integration

The price war has shown signs of promoting integration in this crowded industry. The growth of the industry is largely promoted by the government's strong incentive measures, and these incentive measures are now being canceled rapidly.

With the continuation of the price war, the leaders of large companies are becoming more and more stable, while smaller companies are facing a downturn in sales. According to the China Passenger Car Market Information Joint Meeting(Cpca)In the first four months of this year, BYD, Tesla and GAC Ean's three companies in the pure electric vehicle market increased by 50.1%, higher than 42.7%of the same period last year. BYD led a market share of 24.9%, an increase of 7.4 percentage points year -on -year.

As large brands get more market share, many small brands have continued to lose their markets. Xiaopeng Automobile is the representative of this group. It fell out of the top 10 ranking of electric vehicle manufacturers in the first four months of this year, which is symbolic. Weilai Automobile's market share increased by 0.3 percentage points, but its 27.1%of the increase in car delivery increased far behind BYD and Tesla, because the latter two recorded more than 60%of the year -on -year increase.

Facing the slowdown of growth, it is not surprising that Weilai Automobile's joining the price war is not surprising. But whether this will increase its sales significantly, it remains to be observed.

Xiaopeng's experience is the opposite. The company's significant price reduction in January failed to boost sales. In the first three months of this year, the company's total car delivery volume actually decreased by 47.3%.

Another smaller electric vehicle startup Zero Running Motors also recorded the same bleak performance after launching a large price reduction measure. According to its latest quarterly report, the company's car delivery volume in the first quarter decreased by 51.3%to 10,509 vehicles.

Not all small -scale companies have been affected. In the intensified price war, the ideal car was the last persistence -52,584 vehicles were delivered in the first quarter, a year -on -year increase of 65.8%. During this period, the company also recorded a net profit of 934 million yuan to make it one of the few profitable electric vehicle manufacturers. BYD and Tesla were recorded during this period, while Weilai Automobile, Xiaopeng Automobile and Zero Running cars suffered losses.

The poor performance of small companies is also reflected in their profit margins that lag far behind large -scale peers. The gross profit margin of Weilai, Xiaopeng and Zero in the first quarter was lower than 2%, far lower than BYD's 17.9%, and Tesla's 19.3%higher number.

This pulls back to the dilemma facing the smaller company is now, and they will find that it is increasingly difficult to launch a long -term price war, because it will consume their cash reserves that are constantly shrinking, and investors with skeptical attitudes are not too much. It may provide new funds. As of the end of March, Weilai's cash shrunk from 45.5 billion yuan three months ago to 37.8 billion yuan, while Xiaopeng's cash was reduced from 38 billion yuan to 34 billion yuan in the same period. If the price war continues, the reduction of cash may continue or even accelerate.

The price war has brought some of the smallest major electric vehicle manufacturers on the verge of bankruptcy. Weimar Automobile is one of them. This company was once ambitious and now faces a financial crisis. According to reports, it has greatly reduced employee wages at the end of last year and 2023 and laid a large -scale layoff. Data from CPCA showed that Weimar Automobile sold only 457 vehicles in the first two months of 2023, a year -on -year decrease of 92.4%.

We are reducing risks and diversification. "

Brinken also said that the trip also specifically mentioned to China the US citizen citizen and people who faced outbound banned by the Chinese side, and said they would continue to work hard to ensure that they were released and returned to the United States safely.

There are more high -level interviewers in the United States and China: bilateral relations are still difficult

According to a statement issued by the US State Department spokesman Matthewmiller on the 19th, the two parties emphasized that the United States and China should work together to deal with the common transnational challenges such as climate change, global macroeconomic stability, and anti -drug. The two sides also agreed to restore personnel exchanges and will increase direct flights between the two countries. In addition, Qin Gang agreed to accept the invitation of Brincken to return to Washington at the right time of each other and continue to discuss. The United States also welcomes Chinese officials to visit the United States further.

However, Bonnieglaser, director of the Asian project in the German Marshall Foundation in the United States, also pointed out that it should not exaggerate the results of this trip, because the future relationship is still facing many difficulties.

She specifically pointed out that in Wang Yi's statement, China clearly pushed all the responsibilities of the deterioration of US -China relations to the United States: "This is not the basis for us to stabilize each other's relationship. The United States cannot accept such an interpretation. The signal still exists. In the future, these will still be a challenge. "

Focus on Uyghur | Elixi: NAN (馕) -The eternal theme of Uyghur food culture

A Uyghur hawker in Beijing's "Xinjiang Village" sells newly released 馕 Agence France-Presse information picture Audio-Link: https://www.rfa.org/mandarin/pinglun/jujiaoweiwuer/ylxt -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT -YLXT 06192023120246.html/@streamRecently, Twitter has caused fierce disputes between overseas Uighurs and some Chinese. For more than a week, the controversy continues to ferment.

In the photos that caused controversy, a Ms. Han lady hollowed out the middle of the cricket and hung the collar on the neck; the Uyghur people who saw the photo thought it was a great disrespect, and the Han people thought it was a small Uyghur topic.

Uighurs have a proverb. When the Uyghur people accused those who were arrogant and ignorant and short -sighted, they would say, "With two crickets, knock one as a hand drum." It means that when you eat your stomach, you will start arrogant.

The Han people also have a proverb: "Do not do good but not to do it, do not use evil for small"

Cultural differences are small things in outsiders, but it is a big deal for the people of the personnel; it is a big deal for the Uyghur to hang the hollowing the collar around the neck. Great disrespect. Not only is disrespect for the symbol of Uyghur food culture -馕, but also disrespect to the Uyghur traditional culture.

Because 馕 occupies extremely important positions in the Uyghur diet and traditional culture, and the current Uyghur's racial and cultural extermination of the Chinese colonial government's racial and cultural extermination, which is currently encountered by the Uighurs, is also a cherished food that the Uighur is very cherished. As a gimmicky behavior, it is equivalent to the Uyghur in the suffering.

Overseas Uighurs have been cut off for a few years with their hometown. I do n’t know that parents and relatives are dead, nor do they get any information about relatives and friends. They live in my hometown every day, miss their loved ones, remember the past and work hard to save the traditional Uyghur traditional culture overseas. In the difficulties, it is difficult to restrain your anger in seeing such photos of this kind of desecration of Uyghur traditional food culture.

For Uighurs, 人 (food), salt, and water are extremely precious. The Uighurs have respect and cherish from the inner heart for the inner heart. The Uyghur's respect for tadpoles, salt and water is first of all from a deep understanding and cherishment of their fragile environment.

One of the old Uighurs I heard from a young age is: "馕 is the partner of the journey." The Uyghur's cricket can be stored for a long time after a little air drying. The Uyghur's preparation for travelers generally use milk, butter, sesame and other grilled. Even if it is stored for a long time, as long as it is put in milk tea or water, it will be soft instantly; The first choice of essential food.

Children must travel long, and parents and relatives will inevitably bake the fresh Toghach (Xiaoyuan 馕) that is convenient to carry.

I am the late father, and it can be said that it is a master of baked. After his father lost his parents since he was a child, his relatives were sent to Master Kashgar Bakery as an apprentice, and later participated in the National Army of the East Turkestan (Xinjiang Uygur Autonomous Region), and was assigned to the cooking class to be responsible for a soldier's diet. Continue to bake for the National Army soldiers. Later, he was transferred to the railway as a worker, but he always liked to roast it at home.

I went to college for five years. Before I returned to school, my father would bake me small oil for two or three days in advance; bake baked buns one day in the winter vacation. Later, my classmates knew that I must have a special small oil and baked buns that I had to bake in school. Every time I returned to school, I took my classmates the most; when I returned to the dormitory, everyone sat on the table and ate roasted. Buns and small oils, talking about the endless talk of hometown. That scene expresses our infinite nostalgia and love for our hometown.

Later, after graduating and working, I always felt that I always felt too much. After returning to Yili to visit my grandparents, I returned to Shihezi. My grandmother said that she wanted to bake off, and I resolutely refused; I told my grandmother that I could buy it everywhere, and there was no need to bring it. But grandma still baked a small oil -filled carton. In order to prevent grandpa and grandma from being sad, I was reluctant to take a small box of oil.

When I went to Ili to live in a relative's house, I got up the next morning, I deliberately forgotten the oil at relatives' house, hurriedly came to the long -distance bus station of Yili World, and opened the station at 9 o'clock; more than an hour later, I came to Bayanyu When I had breakfast, I found that my wallet was gone. I turned left and right. I had nothing except tickets and a travel bag. Gu Gui, no one who knew the car had to sit hungry; I was in my heart, as long as I could go to Shihezi that day, I would be hungry for a day!

What is not smooth and everything is not smooth. When I go to the Guozigou bus, I am thinking that the driver can repair the car as soon as possible and drive to Shihezi at night. However, it was in the afternoon when the car was repaired; obviously, I could not arrive at Shihezi that night.

I pray that the car can go to Jinghe or Wusu earlier. I have friends in these two places. As long as you arrive before dark, I can find friends to borrow money. But it was dark soon, and the car did not stop in Jinghe. I started to look forward to the rain. As long as it does not rain, it should not be difficult one night in Wusu; however, when the house leaks in the rain, when the car enters the Wusu Passenger Station, it starts the wind and rain outside.

I was hungry and tired, and ran into a Uyghur restaurant near the station with a backpack. A pair of Uyghur husbands were dining. I told them that I was a teacher of Shi Hezi, lost their wallets, and were willing to sell watches, or suit on the body; My suit asked how much money me sells, I told him 10 yuan. I just want to have a place to live, if you may eat a bowl of rice.

I am about to take off the suit and let the young man look at it. His wife cannot speak doubt: "Who is not in trouble, not to mention that this gentleman is still a teacher. Take it out in the pocket. "In this way, the couple took me to a hotel next to the passenger station to help me pay for the accommodation; Hungry and unable to fall asleep; all night, the sound of the rain hit the window in the ear, and the gurgling sound of the stomach, and the little oil was boiled in front of her grandmother. Intersection

That night, for the first time, I realized the meaning of the ancient proverb of "Journey to the Travel". Since then, I have never rejected my grandparents, or the roasting of my grandparents, or my parents and siblings.

Even in the United States, as long as it is possible, I will bring it on long -distance travel.

Just two weeks ago, I drove to Maryland to meet. The meeting with a colleague was over before noon, but we must leave the meeting with another group of three colleagues. Their meeting was delayed until three pm to end before the end EssenceI asked my colleagues if it was a bit hard and liked, he said it was particularly delicious; I said it was the Uyghur's cricket; I intended to lead the topic to Uyghur topic; beyond me, he said that he knew the Uyghur and also ate it. Passing the Uyghur's cricket; of course, he also knows the racial extinction we are currently encountered. Half a piece, and the distance between me and my colleagues closer again. On the way, we talked a lot.

For Uighurs, 人 is not only a journey partner, but also an important part of Uyghur traditional culture; 馕 and salt are also the most important part of the Uyghur marriage ceremony. Men and women who are about to become husbands and wives. After the religious person hosts the wedding ceremony, someone will definitely bring a small bowl of salt water soaked in salt water. Both men and women should eat them together, indicating that the two sides will be loyal and never separated.

传 and Salt are also sacred certificates used by traditional Uyghurs to swear. In the case of major events or accused, the oath or the accused will vow to prove that they are telling the truth in the sore and salt, and they will not lie.

Uyghur children have been educated by parents and teachers since childhood to respect, salt and water. If you want to eat it, you must not take the whole piece of crickets. You have to open it. Eat a small piece and a small piece to avoid ca n’t be a waste; Repent; if you see a block that falls on the ground on the road, be sure to pick it up and put it on a high place, or feed poultry and livestock.

Alas, it is also one of the must bring gifts for Uighurs to visit relatives and friends. So far, the rural and some cities Uighurs visit relatives and friends. Ladies generally bring their own freshly baked fresh and visit relatives and friends.

Alas, it is also the first important food for Uighurs to receive guests. The family of inviting guests generally bake the hobby of the guests first; to welcome the 馕 at the guest table, it must be a fresh whole piece; after welcome the guests into the house, the owner first respects the tea (clear tea or milk tea), and then The owner will make the whole puppet into a few pieces to ask the guests to drink tea; after that, it is the other traditional food.

The Uyghur educating children cannot pour garbage and dust into the water, let alone urinate in the water; wash your hands and wash your face and wash your face. You must use a kettle. You cannot wash the clothes from the river and the canal.

When I was in school at the Hami Railway, I made a pull strip at home. The water below, because of salt, parents asked us not to pour the noodle soup into the garbage dump and the soil road in front of the door to avoid being stepped on; This was the one I had the most headache.

Obviously, these taboos of the Uyghur are not unreasonable dogma, but the care of the Uyghur's environment from the Uighurs, which stems from respect for nature!

Of course, modern life has changed us and the Uighurs have also changed; but the Uyghur's nostalgia and respect for salt, salt, and water has not changed; and from the perspective of modern environmental protection, we look back at the Uighur tradition. It is necessary to change, and it should be more promoted.

has been chased and killed since 1988

A photo of Rashdi in 1986
