Videos: []

Images: ["000000.png"]

The election committee officially approved the voting results of the 500 seats of the House of Representatives, making the Move FORWARD PARTY (MFP) that won 151 seats became the largest party.

Pita Limjaroenrat, the leader of the Party, is a strong candidate for the Prime Minister, although he is facing an investigation that may make him qualified.

The Election Commission is investigating about 200 complaints on the May 14th election.

The Secretary -General of the Election Commission Sawang Boonmee said at a press conference: "We decided to announce the approval of the election results because not all complaints can be handled within 60 days."

Thailand law stipulates that the election results need to be approved within 60 days, but the election committee can investigate complaint cases for one year.

The parliament will hold a meeting within 15 days and choose the Speaker of the House of Representatives. When the new Prime Minister is elected, there is no fixed timetable.

The APPC said that it has alliances with the 2nd largest party including the second largest party (PHEU THAI), which will allow them to occupy a majority of seats in the House of Representatives.

However, in order to ensure the position of the Prime Minister, Pitta needs to win a majority support in the two hospitals, including the Senate selected by 250 seats by the previous military government.

Last week, Pitta encountered the latest setbacks. The Election Commission set up a special committee to investigate whether he was qualified to run for public office.

The investigation involves the issue of Pitta's ITV that has been dissolved in the current media company. According to Thai law, those who hold media shares cannot run. If he is sentenced to guilty, he may be disqualified and faces a maximum 10 -year imprisonment.

Pitta said he inherited ITV shares after his father's death, and ITV stopped operating in 2007.

Because voters rejected Prayut Chan-O-Cha CHA, who had rejected the commander-in-chief of the Army and launched a coup in 2014, the Thai party who won 141 seats in this election occupied the upper hand in this election.

Anwar is also the Minister of Finance. He was in Malaysia Securities Supervision on Monday ...

Videos: []

Audios: []

Images: []

Type: NewsArticle

Breadcrumbs: ['即时', '国际']

Keywords: ['安华', '股市', '马来西亚', '上市']

The Malaysian stock market and the Limori currency value has continued to decline recently. Prime Minister Anwar Anhua announced on Monday (June 19) that three new measures to revitalize stock markets include reducing stock stamp duty, simplify listing procedures, and promote corporate investment.

Anwar is also the Minister of Finance. He attended the "CMGP Promotion Ceremony" at the Malaysian Securities Supervision Committee on Monday at the Malaysian Securities Supervision Committee that starting on July 1, the stamp tax rate of stock transactions will be reduced from 0.15%to 0.10%. The maximum limit of the stamp duty of each contract on July 1 is RM1,000 (about S $ 290).

He said that lowering the printing duty will directly reduce the cost of securities transaction, stimulate and enhance market attractiveness, which makes Malaysian stock market more competitive.

In terms of simplifying listing procedures, Anhua said: "I think the capital market and economic transformation of Malaysia need long -term market and structural reform. As a start, the government will encourage more enterprises to go public on the Malaysia Stock Exchange. The Malaysian Exchange will implement reform this year, speed up the approval procedures for the first public sales (IPO), and shorten the time of listing.

He pointed out that after the implementation of these measures, it will become easier and faster to be listed on the Malaysian Stock Exchange, which will ensure the competitiveness and attractiveness of Malaysia.

He said that the increase in market flow will attract more domestic and foreign funds to enter the Malaysian stock market, and encourage small and medium -sized enterprises (SME) to sell for the first time. He said that this can also promote the expansion of the business scale of listed companies, create more employment opportunities, expand investor groups, and promote the structural reform of the Malaysian capital market.

As for the investment in enterprise, Anhua announced: "In order to attract more investors to support the financing of SMEs and new economies, the Ministry of Finance and the Securities Supervision Committee will study how to promote and attract policies to promote and attract family offices in Malaysia. Will study and promote corporate venture capital plans, and promote more domestic direct investment through more preferential taxation and incentive policies. "

He said that the Ministry of Finance and the Securities Supervision Committee will also expand the definition of mature investors, which will cover angel investors, risk capitalists and private equity companies.

In summary, Anhua pointed out that these three new measures to boost the vitality and attractiveness of Malaysia's capital market are formulated by the Ministry of Finance and the Securities Regulatory Commission according to the feedback from the Malaysian exchanges and the stock market -related industries.

He said that the government hopes that the above three new policies will increase market vitality and increase the attractiveness of the Malaysian capital market. At the same time, they will expand people's investment and wealth creation opportunities, attract more investors to support SME financing and new economy, and implement them and implement them. Market and structural reforms to restore investors' confidence in the vitality and competitiveness of the Malaysian market.

He emphasized: "Any reform requires discipline and patience, and the government also needs confidence and courage to try new things to make difficult decisions for the people and national interests."

North Korea's error is the "most serious failure" of the spy satellite launch

Author: 通讯社

Publisher: Al Jazeera

Published Time: 2023-06-19T3:02:42

Modified Time: 2023-06-19T08:17:38

Description: After the "severe criticism" who was responsible for the first failure test, the Labor Party officials promised to successfully launch a spy satellite as soon as possible.

Images: ["1-1687161159.jpg", "2-1687161176.jpg"]

Topics: ['军事', '政治', '新闻']

Keywords: ['军事', '政治', '新闻', '朝鲜']

Type: Article

North Korean leader Kim Jong -un (middle) at the party meeting(Reuters)According to official media reports, senior North Korean officials have promised to try to launch military spy satellites again, and call the first launch test of their country's failure last month as the "worst failure" this year.

According to a report from the DPRK, the promise was made at the administrative North Korean Workers' Party Conference held on Friday to Sunday.

The North Korean Society stated that the expansion of all conferences require staff and researchers to analyze the reasons for the failure of the launch, and "severely criticize" the person who is responsible for the mistake.

North Korea tried to send its first military spy satellite into the orbit on May 31, but due to the rocket failure in Pyongyang, the aircraft and its effective load fell into the sea shortly after the launch.

The largest on -site fire exercise in the history of the United States and South Korea(Peninsula TV Station)The crash has led North Korea leader Kim Jong -un to obtain the heavenly foundation surveillance system to better monitor the efforts of the United States and South Korea.

Washington and Seoul condemned the launch on May 31st, saying that it violated the United Nations resolution that banned Pyongyang from using ballistic missile technology to conduct any test. Analysts pointed out that there is a significant technology overlap between the development of intercontinental ballistic missiles and the capacity of space launch.

The report from the North Korean Society did not specifically explain that North Korea might try to make the second launch date. However, the Korean spy agency told the legislators earlier that Pyongyang may need "more than a few weeks" to determine what the first experiment was.

South Korea said today that it has successfully salvaged a large piece of wreckage of crashed rockets from Haidilao. Seoul spent more than two weeks for salvage, because these fragments can help scientists understand Pyongyang's ballistic missiles and satellite surveillance programs.

"major progress"

Kim Jong -un has promised to obtain several high -tech military assets to cope with the hostile operations of his so -called American as the United States. This spy satellite is one of the one. In addition, multi -warhead missiles, nuclear submarines, and solid propulsion intercontinental ballistic missiles and hypersonic missiles are also other weapon systems that Kim Jong -un wanted to own.

Since the beginning of 2022, North Korea has conducted more than 100 missiles, including some of them related to the spy satellite on the development of Kim Jong -un and other powerful weapons.

In April, North Korea tested the solid fuel intercontinental ballistic missile for the first time. The fuel of this missile has been installed in it, so they are more mobility than rockets using liquid pushing agents, and it is more difficult for outsiders to find before launch.

According to the North Korean Society, during the Labor Party's meeting, members of the Politburo claimed that "major progress" was made in the efforts to expand North Korea's nuclear weapons and missiles, and they claimed that this provided support for the government and the enemy's "positive confrontation" policy.

The report pointed out that members of the Politburo also analyzed the "reckless war move" due to its competitors, which caused the region to "extremely deteriorate the security situation", which obviously refers to the expanding US -South Korea military exercises.

It is reported that they have unanimously approved the unsatisfactory counterattack plan.

According to the DPRK, members of the Politburo of North Korea have formulated "important tasks" that have not been explained in detail, aiming to defend national interests and strengthen the unity of countries that "oppose the strategy of American robbers' world hegemony".

The meeting also discussed that the food supply can be self -sufficient by increasing the national agricultural output and completing the annual grain production goals.

Earlier this year, the South Korean Ministry of Unity stated that the food situation in North Korea "seemed to deteriorate."

This isolated country has been strictly sanctioned due to its nuclear weapons and ballistic missile programs. In addition, the country's economic situation is further nervous because of the strict border blockade of the new crown epidemic.

In addition, the North Korean Society reported that Jin Yingzhe, who had previously served as the Minister of the United Front Department and Kim Jong -un, was appointed as an alternate member of the Political Bureau of the Party Central Committee.

A Korean legislator said at the time that Kim Yingzhe was degraded after failing to reach an agreement with the US summit in 2019. He led the summit negotiations with the then American colleagues and former US Secretary of State Mike Pompeo.
